Build pieces

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/getting-started/introduction#-why-activepieces-is-different)

🔥 Why Activepieces is Different:
=======================================================================================================================================

*   **💖 Loved by Everyone**: Intuitive interface and great experience for both technical and non-technical users with a quick learning curve.

![](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/templates.gif?s=076362bc114929ee518e20251d901b17)

*   **🌐 Open Ecosystem:** All pieces are open source and available on npmjs.com, **60% of the pieces are contributed by the community**.
*   **🛠️ Pieces are written in Typescript**: Pieces are npm packages in TypeScript, offering full customization with the best developer experience, including **hot reloading** for **local** piece development on your machine. 😎

![](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP/resources/create-action.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP&q=85&s=fb6b48d36b7deb67a7ba801a6780a8b6)

*   **🤖 AI-Ready**: Native AI pieces and agents are built into Activepieces. Integrating AI into your flows is seamless and simple—experiment with popular providers, or quickly create custom agents using our easy-to-use AI SDK.
*   **🏢 Enterprise-Ready**: Developers set up the tools, and anyone in the organization can use the no-code builder. Full customization from branding to control.
*   **🔒 Secure by Design**: Self-hosted and network-gapped for maximum security and control over your data.
*   **🧠 Human in Loop**: Delay execution for a period of time or require approval. These are just pieces built on top of the piece framework, and you can build many pieces like that. 🎨

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/overview/welcome.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/overview/welcome)

[Building Flows](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/building-flows)

About

License

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

Activepieces’ **core** is released as open source under the [MIT license](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/blob/main/LICENSE)
 and enterprise / cloud editions features are released under [Commercial License](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/blob/main/packages/ee/LICENSE)
 The MIT license is a permissive license that grants users the freedom to use, modify, or distribute the software without any significant restrictions. The only requirement is that you include the license notice along with the software when distributing it. Using the enterprise features (under the packages/ee and packages/server/api/src/app/ee folder) with a self-hosted instance requires an Activepieces license. If you are looking for these features, contact us at [\[email protected\]](https://www.activepieces.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#3d4e5c51584e7d5c5e49544b584d54585e584e135e5250)
. **Benefits of Dual Licensing Repo**

*   **Transparency** - Everyone can see what we are doing and contribute to the project.
*   **Clarity** - Everyone can see what the difference is between the open source and commercial versions of our software.
*   **Audit** - Everyone can audit our code and see what we are doing.
*   **Faster Development** - We can develop faster and more efficiently.

If you are still confused or have feedback, please open an issue on GitHub or send a message in the #contribution channel on Discord.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/about/license.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/about/license)

# Setup AI Providers - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/setup-ai-providers#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Guides

Setup AI Providers

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Supported Providers](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/setup-ai-providers#supported-providers)
    
*   [How to Setup](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/setup-ai-providers#how-to-setup)
    
*   [Cost Control & Logging](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/setup-ai-providers#cost-control-%26-logging)
    

AI providers are configured by the platform admin to centrally manage credentials and access, making [AI pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/pieces/ai)
 and their features available to everyone in all projects.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/setup-ai-providers#supported-providers)

Supported Providers
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **OpenAI**
*   **Anthropic**
*   **Gemini**
*   **Vercel AI Gateway**
*   **Cloudflare AI Gateway**

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/setup-ai-providers#how-to-setup)

How to Setup
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Go to **Admin Console** → **AI** page. Add your provider’s base URL and API key. These settings apply to all projects. ![Manage AI Providers](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP/resources/screenshots/configure-ai-provider.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP&q=85&s=9bf447af05f4b1358f88d11a8bd23f94)

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/setup-ai-providers#cost-control-&-logging)

Cost Control & Logging
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use an AI gateway like **Vercel AI Gateway** or **Cloudflare AI Gateway** to:

*   Set rate limits and budgets
*   Log and monitor all AI requests
*   Track usage across projects

Just set the gateway URL as your provider’s base URL in the Admin Console.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/setup-ai-providers.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/setup-ai-providers)

[Override OAuth2 Apps](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-oauth2)
[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview)

⌘I

# Overview - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#content-area)

Navigation

Secret Managers

Overview

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Benefits](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#benefits)
    
*   [Supported Providers](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#supported-providers)
    
*   [How to Connect](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#how-to-connect)
    
*   [Connection Scopes](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#connection-scopes)
    
*   [Using Secret Managers in Connection Dialogs](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#using-secret-managers-in-connection-dialogs)
    
*   [How It Works](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#how-it-works)
    
*   [Caching](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#caching)
    
*   [Security Considerations](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#security-considerations)
    
*   [Troubleshooting](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#troubleshooting)
    

Secret Managers allow you to integrate external secret management systems with Activepieces, enabling centralized credential management and enhanced security for your global connections.

This feature is available in our paid editions. Contact us [here](https://www.activepieces.com/sales)
, and we'll be delighted to assist you!

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#benefits)

Benefits
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Centralized Management**: Store all credentials in one secure location
*   **Enhanced Security**: Credentials are managed by dedicated secret management systems
*   **Audit & Compliance**: Track access and changes to secrets
*   **Rotation Support**: Easily rotate credentials without updating flows
*   **Access Control**: Use your existing secret manager access policies

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#supported-providers)

Supported Providers
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **[HashiCorp Vault](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/hashicorp)
    ** - Enterprise-grade secrets management
*   **[CyberArk Conjur](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur)
    ** - Centralized secrets management with host-based authentication
*   **[AWS Secrets Manager](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws)
    ** - Managed secrets storage on AWS
*   **[1Password](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword)
    ** - Consumer and team password manager with Secrets Automation

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#how-to-connect)

How to Connect
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to **Platform Admin → Security → Secret Managers**
2.  Click **New Connection**
3.  Select the secret manager provider you want to connect
4.  Enter a **Name** for the connection
5.  Choose a **Scope** (see [Connection Scopes](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#connection-scopes)
     below)
6.  Follow the provider-specific setup instructions in the provider documentation
7.  Enter the required connection details
8.  Click **Save** to test and save the connection

The connection will be encrypted and stored securely. You can edit or delete it at any time from the Secret Managers page.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#connection-scopes)

Connection Scopes
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each secret manager connection has a **scope** that controls which projects can use it:

| Scope | Description |
| --- | --- |
| **Platform** | Available to all projects on the platform |
| **Project** | Restricted to specific projects you select |

When creating or editing a connection, select **Project** scope and choose the projects that should have access. Platform-scoped connections are always visible to all projects.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#using-secret-managers-in-connection-dialogs)

Using Secret Managers in Connection Dialogs
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once connected, you can reference secrets from your secret managers when configuring piece connections:

1.  Open a connection dialog (either a global connection or one inside the flow builder)
2.  Click the **key icon** (🔑) next to a credential field
3.  Select a secret manager connection from the dropdown
4.  Enter the secret path/identifier required by your provider (see provider-specific documentation)
5.  The connection will automatically retrieve the secret from your secret manager when needed

**Global connections (Platform Admin):** All platform-scoped and project-scoped secret manager connections are available to select. **Flow builder connections:** Only secret manager connections that are accessible to the current project are shown — this includes platform-scoped connections and project-scoped connections assigned to that project. ![Manage Oauth2 apps](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/yqMjtHswhi3w4D2R/resources/screenshots/secret-manager.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=yqMjtHswhi3w4D2R&q=85&s=608015daeff79c8368a12c5fa2d488e0)

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#how-it-works)

How It Works
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you use a secret manager in a connection:

*   The global connection stores a reference to the secret (not the actual credential)
*   When the flow runs, Activepieces authenticates with your secret manager and retrieves the secret
*   Secrets are fetched on-demand and never stored in Activepieces
*   If the secret is updated in your secret manager, flows will use the new value after the cache expires (up to 1 hour), or immediately after clearing the cache

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#caching)

Caching
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Connection checks and retrieved secrets are cached in Redis (encrypted) for **1 hour** to reduce latency and provider API load. To force a refresh (e.g. after rotating credentials or updating secrets), platform admins can clear the cache per connection using the **refresh icon** next to each connection row in the Secret Managers page. ![Clear secret manager cache](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/4VmBz4sovrlimK2J/resources/screenshots/clear-secret-manager-cache.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=4VmBz4sovrlimK2J&q=85&s=eeea58560084b3808ee9bbc26b433aab) You can also clear the cache via the API. Omit `connectionId` to clear all cached entries for the platform, or pass a `connectionId` to clear only that connection’s cache:

    # Clear cache for a specific connection
    curl --request DELETE \
      --url 'https://<domain>/api/v1/secret-managers/cache?connectionId=<connectionId>' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>'
    
    # Clear all platform cache entries
    curl --request DELETE \
      --url 'https://<domain>/api/v1/secret-managers/cache' \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>'
    

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#security-considerations)

Security Considerations
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Encryption**: Secret managers authentication configuration is encrypted
*   **Access Control**: Use your secret manager’s access policies to control who can access secrets
*   **Network Security**: Ensure your secret manager is accessible from your Activepieces instance
*   **Credential Management**: Regularly rotate authentication credentials for secret managers

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Connection Failed:**

*   Verify the connection details are correct and accessible
*   Check that authentication credentials are valid
*   Ensure network connectivity between Activepieces and your secret manager
*   Review provider-specific troubleshooting guides

**Secret Not Found:**

*   Verify the secret path/name is correct
*   Check that the secret exists in your secret manager
*   Ensure the authentication credentials have permissions to read the secret

**Permission Denied:**

*   Verify the authentication credentials have the necessary permissions
*   Check your secret manager’s access control policies
*   Review audit logs in your secret manager for detailed error information

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview)

[Setup AI Providers](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/setup-ai-providers)
[AWS Secrets Manager](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws)

⌘I

# How to Setup SSO - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Guides

How to Setup SSO

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)

[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#overview)
    
*   [Prerequisites](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#prerequisites)
    
*   [Accessing SSO Configuration](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#accessing-sso-configuration)
    
*   [Enforcing SSO](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#enforcing-sso)
    
*   [Supported SSO Providers](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#supported-sso-providers)
    
*   [Google](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#google)
    
*   [GitHub](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#github)

*   [SAML with JumpCloud](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#saml-with-jumpcloud)
    
*   [Troubleshooting](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#troubleshooting)
    
*   [Need Help?](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#need-help)
    

This feature is available in our paid editions. Contact us [here](https://www.activepieces.com/sales)
, and we'll be delighted to assist you!

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#overview)

Overview
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Single Sign-On (SSO) allows your team to authenticate using your organization’s existing identity provider, eliminating the need for separate Activepieces credentials. This improves security, simplifies user management, and provides a seamless login experience.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before configuring SSO, ensure you have:

*   **Admin access** to your Activepieces platform
*   **Admin access** to your identity provider (Google, GitHub, Okta, or JumpCloud)
*   The **redirect URL** from your Activepieces SSO configuration screen

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#accessing-sso-configuration)

Accessing SSO Configuration
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Navigate to **Platform Settings** → **SSO** in your Activepieces admin dashboard to access the SSO configuration screen. ![SSO Configuration](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/screenshots/sso.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-&q=85&s=c4cd4418c83c077bfebbd6d74509d52e)

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#enforcing-sso)

Enforcing SSO
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can enforce SSO by specifying your organization’s email domain. When SSO enforcement is enabled:

*   Users with matching email domains must authenticate through the SSO provider
*   Email/password login can be disabled for enhanced security
*   All authentication is routed through your designated identity provider

We recommend testing SSO with a small group of users before enforcing it organization-wide.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#supported-sso-providers)

Supported SSO Providers
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Activepieces supports multiple SSO providers to integrate with your existing identity management system.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#google)

Google

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Access Google Cloud Console

Go to the [Google Cloud Console](https://console.cloud.google.com/)
 and select your project (or create a new one).

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Create OAuth2 Credentials

Navigate to **APIs & Services** → **Credentials** → **Create Credentials** → **OAuth client ID**.Select **Web application** as the application type.

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Configure Redirect URI

Copy the **Redirect URL** from the Activepieces SSO configuration screen and add it to the **Authorized redirect URIs** in Google Cloud Console.

4

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Copy Credentials to Activepieces

Copy the **Client ID** and **Client Secret** from Google and paste them into the corresponding fields in Activepieces.

5

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Save Configuration

Click **Finish** to complete the setup.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#github)

GitHub

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Access GitHub Developer Settings

Go to [GitHub Developer Settings](https://github.com/settings/developers)
 → **OAuth Apps** → **New OAuth App**.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Register New Application

Fill in the application details:

*   **Application name**: Choose a recognizable name (e.g., “Activepieces SSO”)
*   **Homepage URL**: Enter your Activepieces instance URL

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Configure Authorization Callback

Copy the **Redirect URL** from the Activepieces SSO configuration screen and paste it into the **Authorization callback URL** field.

4

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Complete Registration

Click **Register application** to create the OAuth App.

5

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Generate Client Secret

After registration, click **Generate a new client secret** and copy it immediately (it won’t be shown again).

6

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Copy Credentials to Activepieces

Copy the **Client ID** and **Client Secret** and paste them into the corresponding fields in Activepieces.

7

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Save Configuration

Click **Finish** to complete the setup.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#saml-with-okta)

SAML with Okta

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Create New Application in Okta

Go to the [Okta Admin Portal](https://login.okta.com/)
 → **Applications** → **Create App Integration**.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Select SAML 2.0

Choose **SAML 2.0** as the sign-on method and click **Next**.

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Configure General Settings

Enter an **App name** (e.g., “Activepieces”) and optionally upload a logo. Click **Next**.

4

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Configure SAML Settings

*   **Single sign-on URL**: Copy the SSO URL from the Activepieces configuration screen
*   **Audience URI (SP Entity ID)**: Enter `Activepieces`
*   **Name ID format**: Select `EmailAddress`

5

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Add Attribute Statements

Add the following attribute mappings:

| Name | Value |
| --- | --- |
| `firstName` | `user.firstName` |
| `lastName` | `user.lastName` |
| `email` | `user.email` |

6

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Complete Setup in Okta

Click **Next**, select the appropriate feedback option, and click **Finish**.

7

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Export IdP Metadata

Go to the **Sign On** tab → **View SAML setup instructions** or **View IdP metadata**. Copy the Identity Provider metadata XML.

8

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Configure Activepieces

*   Paste the **IdP Metadata** XML into the corresponding field
*   Copy the **X.509 Certificate** from Okta and paste it into the **Signing Key** field

9

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Save Configuration

Click **Save** to complete the setup.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#saml-with-jumpcloud)

SAML with JumpCloud

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Create New Application in JumpCloud

Go to the [JumpCloud Admin Portal](https://console.jumpcloud.com/)
 → **SSO Applications** → **Add New Application** → **Custom SAML App**.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Configure ACS URL

Copy the **ACS URL** from the Activepieces configuration screen and paste it into the **ACS URLs** field in JumpCloud.![JumpCloud ACS URL](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/screenshots/jumpcloud/acl-url.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-&q=85&s=21d5aae4e46ebd6cfc5611b4d5d30c88)

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Configure SP Entity ID

Set the **SP Entity ID** (Audience URI) to `Activepieces`.

4

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Add User Attributes

Configure the following attribute mappings:

| Service Provider Attribute | JumpCloud Attribute |
| --- | --- |
| `firstName` | `firstname` |
| `lastName` | `lastname` |
| `email` | `email` |

![JumpCloud User Attributes](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/screenshots/jumpcloud/user-attribute.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-&q=85&s=51b3448b758b1e2c90f09646421b87a0)

5

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Enable HTTP-Redirect Binding

JumpCloud does not include the `HTTP-Redirect` binding by default. You **must** enable this option.![JumpCloud Redirect Binding](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/screenshots/jumpcloud/declare-login.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-&q=85&s=5d1e72816ff38b9a77ed29991bf25a57)

Without HTTP-Redirect binding, the SSO integration will not work correctly.

6

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Export Metadata

Click **Save**, then refresh the page and click **Export Metadata**.![JumpCloud Export Metadata](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/screenshots/jumpcloud/export-metadata.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-&q=85&s=b2541f12de981d893e8ea7810ab64dc4)

Verify that the exported XML contains `Binding="urn:oasis:names:tc:SAML:2.0:bindings:HTTP-Redirect"` to ensure the binding was properly enabled.

7

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Configure IdP Metadata in Activepieces

Paste the exported metadata XML into the **IdP Metadata** field in Activepieces.

8

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Configure Signing Certificate

Locate the `<ds:X509Certificate>` element in the IdP metadata and extract its value. Format it as a PEM certificate:

    -----BEGIN CERTIFICATE-----
    [PASTE THE CERTIFICATE VALUE HERE]
    -----END CERTIFICATE-----
    

Paste this into the **Signing Key** field.

9

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Assign Users to Application

In JumpCloud, assign the application to the appropriate users or user groups.![JumpCloud Assign App](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/screenshots/jumpcloud/user-groups.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-&q=85&s=5a829b002dfb0106cf16945b7381cba4)

10

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#)

Save Configuration

Click **Finish** to complete the setup.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Users cannot log in after SSO configuration

*   Verify the redirect URL is correctly configured in your identity provider
*   Ensure users are assigned to the application in your identity provider
*   Check that email domains match the SSO enforcement settings

SAML authentication fails

*   Confirm the IdP metadata is complete and correctly formatted
*   Verify the signing certificate is properly formatted with BEGIN/END markers
*   Ensure all required attributes (firstName, lastName, email) are mapped

HTTP-Redirect binding error (JumpCloud)

*   Enable the HTTP-Redirect binding option in JumpCloud
*   Re-export the metadata after enabling the binding
*   Verify the binding appears in the exported XML

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#need-help)

Need Help?
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you encounter issues during SSO setup, please contact our enterprise support or [sales team](https://www.activepieces.com/sales)
.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/sso)

[How to Manage Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces)
[SCIM Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview)

⌘I

Override OAuth2 Apps

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)

On this page

*   [Default Behavior](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-oauth2#default-behavior)
    
*   [Why Replace OAuth2 Apps?](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-oauth2#why-replace-oauth2-apps)
    
*   [How to Configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-oauth2#how-to-configure)
    

This feature is available in our paid editions. Contact us [here](https://www.activepieces.com/sales)
, and we'll be delighted to assist you!

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-oauth2#default-behavior)

Default Behavior
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When users connect to services like Google Sheets or Slack, they see “Activepieces” as the app requesting access. This works out of the box with no setup required.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-oauth2#why-replace-oauth2-apps)

Why Replace OAuth2 Apps?
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Branding**: Show your company name instead of “Activepieces” in authorization screens
*   **Higher Limits**: Some services have stricter rate limits for shared OAuth apps
*   **Compliance**: Your organization may require using company-owned credentials

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-oauth2#how-to-configure)

How to Configure
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to **Platform Admin → Setup → Pieces**
2.  Find the piece you want to configure (e.g., Google Sheets)
3.  Click the lock icon to open the OAuth2 settings
4.  Enter your own Client ID and Client Secret

![Manage Oauth2 apps](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/screenshots/manage-oauth2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-&q=85&s=33b36a1667c9879a845e9ffa6302678c)

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-oauth2.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/manage-oauth2)

[SCIM with Okta](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta)
[Setup AI Providers](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/setup-ai-providers)

# How to Manage Pieces - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Guides

How to Manage Pieces

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#overview)
    
*   [Platform-Level Management](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#platform-level-management)
    
*   [Project-Level Management](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#project-level-management)
    
*   [Show/Hide Pieces in a Project](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#show%2Fhide-pieces-in-a-project)
    
*   [Install Private Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#install-private-pieces)
    

This feature is available in our paid editions. Contact us [here](https://www.activepieces.com/sales)
, and we'll be delighted to assist you!

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#overview)

Overview
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Pieces** are the building blocks of Activepieces — they are integrations and connectors (like Google Sheets, Slack, OpenAI, etc.) that users can use in their automation flows. As a platform administrator, you have full control over which pieces are available to your users. This allows you to:

*   **Enforce security policies** by restricting access to certain integrations
*   **Simplify the user experience** by showing only relevant pieces for your use case
*   **Deploy custom/private pieces** that are specific to your organization

There are **two levels** of piece management:

| Level | Who Can Manage | Scope |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Platform Level** | Platform Admin | Install and remove across the entire platform |
| **Project Level** | Project Admin | Show/hide specific pieces for specfic project |

* * *

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#platform-level-management)

Platform-Level Management
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Platform administrators can manage pieces for the entire Activepieces instance from **Platform Admin → Setup → Pieces**.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#project-level-management)

Project-Level Management
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Project administrators can further restrict which pieces are available within their specific project. This is useful when different teams or projects need access to different integrations.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#show/hide-pieces-in-a-project)

Show/Hide Pieces in a Project

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#)

Open Project Settings

Navigate to your project and go to **Settings → Pieces**.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#)

Configure Visibility

You’ll see a list of all pieces installed on the platform. Toggle the visibility for each piece:

*   **Enabled**: Users in this project can use the piece
*   **Disabled**: The piece is hidden from users in this project

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#)

Save Changes

Changes take effect immediately — users will only see the enabled pieces when building their flows.

![Manage Pieces](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/screenshots/manage-pieces.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-&q=85&s=ea899782b139f0fa2f5d2a2d481ef256) ![Manage Pieces](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/screenshots/manage-pieces-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-&q=85&s=3e0a74e89a61b988c3f8e84099f8a3a1)

Project-level settings can only **hide** pieces that are installed at the platform level. You cannot add pieces at the project level that aren’t already installed on the platform.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#install-private-pieces)

Install Private Pieces

For detailed instructions on building custom pieces, check the [Building Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
 documentation.

If you’ve built a custom piece for your organization, you can upload it directly as a tarball (`.tgz`) file.

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#)

Build Your Piece

Build your piece using the Activepieces CLI:

    npm run pieces -- build --name=your-piece-name
    

This generates a tarball in `dist/packages/pieces/your-piece-name`.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#)

Navigate to Pieces Settings

Go to **Platform Admin → Setup → Pieces** and click **Install Piece**.

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#)

Select File Upload

Choose **Upload File** as the installation source.

4

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces#)

Upload the Tarball

Select the `.tgz` file from your build output and upload it.

![Install Piece](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/screenshots/install-piece.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-&q=85&s=f0d73c60a5077685d90f537a4f8a4ec1)

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces)

[How to Structure Projects](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[How to Setup SSO](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso)

# i18n Translations - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/about/i18n#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

About

i18n Translations

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Contribute to existing translations](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/about/i18n#contribute-to-existing-translations)
    
*   [Adding a new language](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/about/i18n#adding-a-new-language)
    

This guide helps you understand how to change or add new translations. Activepieces uses Crowdin because it helps translators who don’t know how to code. It also makes the approval process easier. Activepieces automatically sync new text from the code and translations back into the code.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/about/i18n#contribute-to-existing-translations)

Contribute to existing translations
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Create Crowdin account
2.  Join the project [https://crowdin.com/project/activepieces](https://crowdin.com/project/activepieces)
    

![Join Project](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP/resources/crowdin.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP&q=85&s=497c4c227a57393942aced37358b2615)

3.  Click on the language you want to translate
4.  Click on “Translate All”

![Translate All](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP/resources/crowdin-translate-all.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP&q=85&s=7b09feacb0d45bbea605269aad2bf44e)

5.  Select Strings you want to translate and click on “Save” button

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/about/i18n#adding-a-new-language)

Adding a new language
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Please contact us ([\[email protected\]](https://www.activepieces.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#e5969095958a9791a58486918c9380958c80868096cb868a88)
    ) if you want to add a new language. We will add it to the project and you can start translating.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/about/i18n.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/about/i18n)

[Tools Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools)

# SCIM Overview - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

SCIM

SCIM Overview

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [What is SCIM?](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview#what-is-scim)
    
*   [What SCIM Handles](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview#what-scim-handles)
    
*   [SCIM and SSO](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview#scim-and-sso)
    
*   [Supported Providers](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview#supported-providers)
    
*   [Configuration](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview#configuration)
    
*   [Architecture](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview#architecture)
    

This feature is available in our paid editions. Contact us [here](https://www.activepieces.com/sales)
, and we'll be delighted to assist you!

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview#what-is-scim)

What is SCIM?
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

SCIM (System for Cross-domain Identity Management) lets your identity provider automatically create, update, and deactivate users in Activepieces.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview#what-scim-handles)

What SCIM Handles
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Provision users** when they are assigned in your identity provider
*   **Sync profile updates** such as name or email changes
*   **Deprovision users** when access is removed or accounts are deactivated

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview#scim-and-sso)

SCIM and SSO
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

SCIM handles user lifecycle management.  
SSO handles sign-in and authentication. You can use both together so user access is managed centrally in your identity provider.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview#supported-providers)

Supported Providers
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Okta
----

Configure SCIM provisioning from Okta to Activepieces.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview#configuration)

Configuration
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Variable | Description | Default |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `AP_SCIM_DEFAULT_PROJECT_ROLE` | The project role assigned to members when added via SCIM group sync. Accepted values: `Admin`, `Editor`, `Viewer`. | `Editor` |

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview#architecture)

Architecture
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![SCIM Architecture Placeholder](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/screenshots/scim/scim-overview-placeholder.svg)

Replace this placeholder with your final architecture image later. Keep the same image path to avoid doc changes.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview)

[How to Setup SSO](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso)
[SCIM with Okta](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta)

# Manage User Roles - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/permissions#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Guides

Manage User Roles

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Default Roles](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/permissions#default-roles)
    
*   [Custom Roles](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/permissions#custom-roles)
    

This feature is available in our paid editions. Contact us [here](https://www.activepieces.com/sales)
, and we'll be delighted to assist you!

Activepieces utilizes Role-Based Access Control (RBAC) for managing permissions within projects. Each project consists of multiple flows and users, with each user assigned specific roles that define their actions within the project.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/permissions#default-roles)

Default Roles
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Activepieces comes with four standard roles out of the box. The table below shows the permissions for each role:

| Permission | Admin | Editor | Operator | Viewer |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Flows** |     |     |     |     |
| View Flows | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |
| Edit Flows | ✓   | ✓   |     |     |
| Publish / Toggle Flows | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |     |
| **Runs** |     |     |     |     |
| View Runs | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |
| Retry Runs | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |     |
| **Connections** |     |     |     |     |
| View Connections | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |
| Edit Connections | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |     |
| **Team** |     |     |     |     |
| View Project Members | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   | ✓   |
| Add/Remove Project Members | ✓   |     |     |     |
| **Git Sync** |     |     |     |     |
| Configure Git Repo | ✓   |     |     |     |
| Pull Flows from Git | ✓   |     |     |     |
| Push Flows to Git | ✓   |     |     |     |

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/permissions#custom-roles)

Custom Roles
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If the default roles don’t fit your needs, you can create custom roles with specific permissions.

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/permissions#)

Navigate to Project Roles

Go to **Platform Admin** → **Security** → **Project Roles**

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/permissions#)

Create a New Role

Click **Create Role** and give it a name

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/permissions#)

Configure Permissions

Select the specific permissions you want to grant to this role

Custom roles are useful when you need fine-grained control, such as allowing users to view and retry runs without being able to edit flows.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/permissions.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/permissions)

[1Password](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword)
[Event Streaming](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming)

⌘I

# Event Streaming - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Navigation

Guides

Event Streaming

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#overview)
    
*   [Use Cases](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#use-cases)
    
*   [Available Events](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#available-events)
    
*   [Flow Events](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#flow-events)
    
*   [Folder Events](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#folder-events)
    
*   [Connection Events](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#connection-events)
    
*   [User Events](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#user-events)
    
*   [Security Events](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#security-events)
    
*   [How to Configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#how-to-configure)
    
*   [Requirements](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#requirements)
    
*   [Troubleshooting](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#troubleshooting)
    

This feature is available in our paid editions. Contact us [here](https://www.activepieces.com/sales)
, and we'll be delighted to assist you!

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#overview)

Overview
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Event Streaming allows you to configure webhook destinations that receive real-time notifications when specific events occur in your Activepieces platform. This enables you to integrate Activepieces with external systems, monitoring tools, analytics platforms, or custom applications.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#use-cases)

Use Cases
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Monitoring & Analytics**: Track flow executions, user activity, and system changes in real-time
*   **Integration**: Sync events with external systems like SIEM tools, data warehouses, or custom dashboards
*   **Compliance**: Maintain audit trails in external systems for compliance requirements
*   **Automation**: Trigger downstream processes based on platform events

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#available-events)

Available Events
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can configure destinations to receive the following event types:

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#flow-events)

Flow Events

*   **Flow Created**: When a new flow is created
*   **Flow Updated**: When a flow is modified
*   **Flow Deleted**: When a flow is removed
*   **Flow Run Started**: When a flow execution begins
*   **Flow Run Finished**: When a flow execution completes
*   **Flow Run Resumed**: When a paused flow execution resumes

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#folder-events)

Folder Events

*   **Folder Created**: When a new folder is created
*   **Folder Updated**: When a folder is modified
*   **Folder Deleted**: When a folder is removed

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#connection-events)

Connection Events

*   **Connection Upserted**: When a connection is created or updated
*   **Connection Deleted**: When a connection is removed

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#user-events)

User Events

*   **User Signed Up**: When a new user registers
*   **User Signed In**: When a user logs in
*   **User Password Reset**: When a password reset is requested
*   **User Email Verified**: When a user verifies their email

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#security-events)

Security Events

*   **Signing Key Created**: When a new signing key is generated
*   **Project Role Created**: When a project role is created
*   **Project Role Updated**: When a project role is modified
*   **Project Role Deleted**: When a project role is removed
*   **Project Release Created**: When a project release is created

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#how-to-configure)

How to Configure
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to **Platform Admin → Infrastructure → Event Destinations**
2.  Click **Create Destination**
3.  Enter your **Webhook URL** (must be a valid HTTPS endpoint)
4.  Select the **Events** you want to receive
5.  Click **Test Destination** to verify the connection (optional)
6.  Click **Create Destination** to save

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#requirements)

Requirements
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Enterprise Edition**: Event Streaming requires an enterprise plan with Audit Logs enabled
*   **HTTPS Endpoint**: Webhook URLs must use HTTPS
*   **Publicly Accessible**: Your endpoint must be accessible from the internet

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Events Not Received**: Verify your endpoint is publicly accessible and returns 2xx status codes
*   **Test Fails**: Check that your URL is valid and uses HTTPS
*   **Missing Events**: Ensure the event type is selected in your destination configuration

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming)

[Manage User Roles](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/permissions)
[Project Releases](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases)

⌘I

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/about/changelog#march-2026)

March 2026

Stability & Reliability Improvements

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/about/changelog#stability-&-reliability-improvements)

Stability & reliability improvements

Major investments in worker architecture, testing, and resilience to ensure more reliable flow execution.**Worker Architecture**

*   Complete worker rewrite (worker v2) focused on stability and reliability
*   New sandbox process model with improved error handling and resource cleanup

**Testing & Quality — what we added and why it matters**Race condition tests:

*   **Queue dispatcher** (12 tests) — tests orphaned job handling when a job is dequeued but all waiters have timed out, prevents double-loop spawn during close with in-flight dequeue, verifies single dequeue concurrency control, tests waiter timeout and retry behavior
*   **Subflow resume** (8 tests) — tests the race condition where the engine writes pause metadata to Redis before it’s persisted to DB, verifies Redis fallback when DB is stale, simulates concurrent reads/writes with spy mocks, covers sync endpoint with concurrent Redis updates
*   **Rate limiter** (5+ tests) — tests concurrent job slot allocation, idempotency with concurrent dispatch, per-project isolation so different projects don’t interfere
*   **Concurrent flow execution** — end-to-end test creating 5 concurrent flow runs verifying none get stuck or deadlocked
*   **Memory lock** — verifies mutual exclusion (two concurrent lock acquire calls on same key are serialized)

Worker unit tests:

*   **Worker polling** — tests job execution lifecycle, resilience to invalid job data, null polls, unrecognized job types, mixed valid/invalid sequences
*   **Sandbox execution** — tests sandbox creation, startup, RPC communication, stdout/stderr accumulation, resource cleanup on timeout or memory issues, process cleanup and listener removal
*   **Process forking** — tests execArgv configuration (memory limits, node options), environment variable propagation
*   **Cache logic** — tests cache hit/miss, disk persistence, memory caching, cache invalidation predicates
*   **Configuration** — tests config loading for different container types (WORKER\_AND\_APP vs WORKER)

End-to-end validation:

*   **[Smoke tests](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/blob/main/.github/workflows/smoke-test.yml)
     in GitHub Actions** — validates health checks and webhook flow execution on AMD64 and ARM64
*   **[Benchmark tests](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/blob/main/.github/workflows/benchmark.yml)
     in GitHub Actions** — load testing across 6 app/worker configurations measuring throughput, mean latency, P50, P99 ([see results](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/benchmark)
    )

**Resilience**

*   Worker gracefully handles invalid job data, null polls, and unrecognized job types
*   Sandbox properly cleans up processes, listeners, and resources on timeout or memory issues
*   Race condition fixes for subflow resume and user interaction jobs

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/about/changelog#march-2026-2)

March 2026

Platform Admin

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/about/changelog#platform-admin-%E2%80%94-full-ui-redesign)

Platform Admin — full UI redesign

A comprehensive visual refresh across all Platform Admin and Project pages with a cleaner, more consistent interface.**Platform Admin**

*   **Projects** — filter chips, inline edit icons, and cleaner sidebar without branding
*   **Users** — new Role and Last Active columns, dedicated Invite button, and per-row action menus
*   **Project Roles** — switched from table to card-based layout with permission viewing
*   **Audit Logs** — fully enabled with Action, Performed By, Project, and Date Range filters, plus detail slide-over panels with a full JSON payload viewer
*   **Secret Managers** — card-based layout with Hashicorp Vault, AWS Secrets Manager, Cyberark Conjur, and 1Password
*   **Branding** — refreshed page layout

**Project pages**

*   **Automations** — renamed from “Flows”, with Type and Owner filters, search, step icon details, status toggles, and favorites
*   **Connections** — Pieces and Owner filters, flow usage count, inline edit and refresh actions
*   **Runs** — updated tab navigation and consistent styling

**General improvements**

*   Unified tab navigation across Automations, Runs, and Connections
*   Platform Admin link added to the bottom of the project sidebar
*   Slide-over panels for detail views instead of full-page navigation
*   Previous / Next pagination style throughout
*   Sidebar header replaced with a “Back to app” link

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/about/changelog#march-2026-3)

March 2026

Staging Environment & Release Process

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/about/changelog#dedicated-staging-environment-&-improved-release-process)

Dedicated staging environment & improved release process

All changes now go through a dedicated staging environment before reaching production. Every update is validated internally for a minimum of 16 hours before being promoted, ensuring higher reliability and fewer disruptions for our users.

*   **Staging-first deployment** — every change is tested in a production-like environment before going live
*   **Daily production promotions** — only validated, stable builds are promoted to production
*   **Weekly self-hosted releases** — predictable, stable releases published every week for self-hosted customers
*   **Emergency hotfix path** — critical fixes can still be fast-tracked to production when needed

[Read more about our release cycle](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/onboarding/release-cycle)

For previous releases, see the [GitHub Releases](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/releases)
 page.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/about/changelog.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/about/changelog)

# SCIM with Okta - Activepieces

, and we'll be delighted to assist you!

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you start, make sure you have:

*   **Admin access** to your Activepieces platform
*   **Admin access** to your Okta tenant
*   SSO already configured (recommended): [SAML with Okta](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#saml-with-okta)
    
*   Generated an API key from `/platform/security/api-keys` route in the Activepieces app

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#configure-scim-connection-in-okta)

Configure SCIM Connection in Okta
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#)

Open your Okta app

In Okta Admin Console, open your Activepieces application (created in [SSO step](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/sso#saml-with-okta)
).

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#)

Enable provisioning

In the app’s **General** tab, enable **SCIM Provisioning**.![Okta User Provisioning Placeholder](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/Jz9nlyeTn6NzuJkR/resources/screenshots/scim/okta/enable-provisioning.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Jz9nlyeTn6NzuJkR&q=85&s=c6c302936ea67358787ebeb2f0085efb)

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#)

Add SCIM connection details

**Provisioning** will be visible, go to it and set:

*   **SCIM base URL** to `https://your-activepieces-domain/api/v1/scim/v2`
*   **Unique identifier field** to `userName`
*   **Authentication mode** to `HTTP Header`
*   **Authorization** to `Bearer <generated-api-key>`

In Supported provisioning actions we support all **Push** actions

4

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#)

Test the connector

Click **Test Connector Configuration** and confirm the test passes.

![Okta SCIM Connection Image](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/Jz9nlyeTn6NzuJkR/resources/screenshots/scim/okta/provisioning.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Jz9nlyeTn6NzuJkR&q=85&s=d5cc1fed46984f574c1de511b88dcdd4)

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#configure-attribute-mapping)

Configure Attribute Mapping
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In **Provisioning -> To App -> Attribute Mappings**, map these fields:

| Activepieces (SCIM) | Okta Value |
| --- | --- |
| `userName` | `user.email` |
| `givenName` | `user.firstName` |
| `familyName` | `user.lastName` |
| `email` | `user.email` |
| `displayName` | `user.displayName` |

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#platform-role-mapping)

Platform role mapping
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, provisioned users will have `Member` role in the platform. In order to specify roles for users in Okta, follow these steps:

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#)

In Okta admin console, navigate to **Directory -> Profile Editor -> Your-Application User**.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#)

Click **Add Attribute** and fill form with:

| Field | Value |
| --- | --- |
| `Display name` | `platformRole` |
| `Variable name` | `platformRole` |
| `External name` | `platformRole` |
| `External namespace` | `urn:ietf:params:scim:schemas:activepieces:1.0:CustomUserAttributes` |
| `Enum` | `enabled` |

For **Attribute members**, add:

| Display name | Value |
| --- | --- |
| `ADMIN` | `ADMIN` |
| `MEMBER` | `MEMBER` |
| `OPERATOR` | `OPERATOR` |

![Okta add attribute image](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/Jz9nlyeTn6NzuJkR/resources/screenshots/scim/okta/add-attribute.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Jz9nlyeTn6NzuJkR&q=85&s=d80e100c6c21ddca7b1abc4e71b4bcb6)Finally click save.

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#)

This step assumes that you already have a field in the Okta user profile that you can map to platformRole in your Activepieces user profile. If you don’t have one, you can create a new field in **Directory -> Profile Editor -> User (default)**.

*   Back to your Activepieces application page in **Provisioning -> To App -> Attribute Mappings**
*   Scroll down and click **Show Unmapped Attributes**
*   Edit `platformRole` field
*   Here you need to map the attribute value from your Okta user profile. If you already have a role field in the Okta user profile that matches exactly with a platformRole value (`ADMIN`, `MEMBER`, `OPERATOR`) then you can select it directly with `Map from Okta Profile` option, otherwise you can use an [Expression](https://developer.okta.com/docs/reference/okta-expression-language/)
     to return one of the 3 roles based on other fields in the Okta user profile.

Here is an example of an expression:![Okta role expression example](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/Jz9nlyeTn6NzuJkR/resources/screenshots/scim/okta/role-expression.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Jz9nlyeTn6NzuJkR&q=85&s=c18b87bea8c5785d5d555df3727726b7)

Please make sure the return value to always be one of `ADMIN`, `MEMBER` or `OPERATOR`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#provision-and-deprovision-users)

Provision and Deprovision Users
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#provision)

Provision

In the Activepieces application page, go to **Provisioning -> To App** and enable the actions you want to be applied to Activepieces when changes occur in Okta. ![Okta role expression example](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/Jz9nlyeTn6NzuJkR/resources/screenshots/scim/okta/provision-actions.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Jz9nlyeTn6NzuJkR&q=85&s=a87b3654367a5488ebf9c1df21a4fb1e) Now in the **Assignments** tab you can:

*   Choose to provision individual users or groups. Note that groups in Okta will be projects in Activepieces.
*   In case you don’t have groups and you want to provision your Okta users at once, you can assign the `Everyone` group.
*   When editing/creating users in an assigned group (including `Everyone`), they should be updated in Activepieces.
*   To push groups to Activepieces, go to the **Push groups** tab and click on the push button, find the group and save.

Default role for users in projects will be `Editor` role, right now there is no way to link the project role with Okta

![Okta role expression example](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/Jz9nlyeTn6NzuJkR/resources/screenshots/scim/okta/push-group.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=Jz9nlyeTn6NzuJkR&q=85&s=103f6e00e03fc97a777549789c1f69f3)

Created users in Activepieces will receive a welcome email. When clicked, they will be redirected to sign in with `SAML`.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#deprovision)

Deprovision

Users’ state switches to `INACTIVE` in Activepieces only when they are deactivated in Okta. Suspension or deletion in Okta does not reflect in Activepieces because of Okta’s design. For groups you can delete them in **Push groups** tab -> click on button in **Push Status** column -> Unlink pushed group -> Delete the group in target

Deleting a group will delete the whole project in Activepieces with its flows and connections. Users linked to that group won’t be affected.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Connector test fails in Okta

*   Confirm SCIM base URL is correct.
*   Ensure the `Authorization` header uses `Bearer` format.

Users are not provisioned

*   Ensure users are assigned to the Okta app.
*   Confirm provisioning actions are enabled in Okta.

Attributes are not updating

*   Recheck mappings in **Provisioning -> To App**.
*   Ensure `userName` uses a stable unique value (usually email).

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/scim/providers/okta)

[SCIM Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/scim/overview)
[Override OAuth2 Apps](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-oauth2)

⌘I
