Project Releases allow you to sync flows, connections, and tables between different projects—essential for teams that want to develop in one environment and deploy to another with confidence.

**Example:** Build and test your automations in a **Staging** project, then seamlessly promote them to **Production** when ready. Simply navigate to your Production project → **Releases** → create a release from Staging, and all your changes will be applied instantly.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#overview)

Overview
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are three ways to create a release:

| Source | Description |
| --- | --- |
| **Git** | Pull changes from a connected Git repository |
| **Project** | Copy flows from another project in your instance |
| **Rollback** | Restore a previous release state |

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#enabling-environments)

Enabling Environments

In your project dashboard, go to settings then to Environments and hit the enable button. ![Enable Environments](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg/resources/screenshots/enable-environments-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg&q=85&s=c2a759e07462c9e7ea01af1176987b96) ![Enable Environments](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg/resources/screenshots/enable-environments-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg&q=85&s=11806d38af71f64d29c9f27ad3f12837)

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#getting-started)

Getting Started
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Navigate to the **Releases** page from your project sidebar to view all releases and create new ones. ![Project Releases Page](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg/resources/screenshots/project-releases-page.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg&q=85&s=97f1f19656a9a1f3923c60d28c062568)

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#connecting-git-optional)

Connecting Git (Optional)
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you want to use Git to track your changes, you’ll need to connect a Git repository first. This requires the Environments feature to be enabled.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#creating-a-release)

Creating a Release
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#from-project)

From Project

Apply changes from flows, connections and tables in one project to another.

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Open Create Release Menu

Click the **Create Release** dropdown button.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Select From Project

Choose **From Project** from the dropdown menu.

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Select Source Project

Choose the project you want to copy flows, connections and tables from.

4

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Review and Apply

Review the changes, and click **Apply Changes**.

![Create Release from Project](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/43FONS7ax8WC7q2h/resources/screenshots/create-release-from-project-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=43FONS7ax8WC7q2h&q=85&s=de30f0867b1a202127ae6925f90c99c2) ![Create Release from Project](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/43FONS7ax8WC7q2h/resources/screenshots/create-release-from-project-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=43FONS7ax8WC7q2h&q=85&s=9e6444bda5b19835f2b4608531e3be13)

New connections created during a release are placeholders and need to be reconnected with valid credentials after the release is applied.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#from-git)

From Git

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Open Create Release Menu

Click the **Create Release** dropdown button.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Select From Git

Choose **From Git** from the dropdown menu.

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Review Changes

A dialog will appear showing all the changes that will be applied:

*   **Flows Changes**: New, updated, or deleted flows
*   **Connections Changes**: New or renamed connections
*   **Tables Changes**: New, updated, or deleted tables

4

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Select Changes

Check or uncheck the flows you want to include in this release.

5

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Add Release Details

Enter a **Name** and optional **Description** for your release.

6

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Apply Changes

Click **Apply Changes** to create the release.

![Create Release from Git](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/43FONS7ax8WC7q2h/resources/screenshots/create-git-release.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=43FONS7ax8WC7q2h&q=85&s=94ae5aecdf6f380294af77f1f2eab362)

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#push-everything-to-git)

Push Everything to Git
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If your project is connected to a Git repository, you can push all your flows, connections, and tables to Git.

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Click Push Everything

Click the **Push Everything** button on the releases page.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Enter Commit Message

Write a descriptive commit message explaining your changes.

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Push

Click **Push** to send all published flows to the Git repository.

![Push Everything to Git Dialog](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg/resources/screenshots/push-everything-to-git.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg&q=85&s=6968bf1e81d51b3b77ab74e0593d8642)

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#pushing-individual-flows-or-tables)

Pushing Individual Flows or Tables
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can also push specific flows or tables to Git without pushing everything.

You can only push published flows to git

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Select Items

Navigate to your flows or tables and select the items you want to push.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Open Push Dialog

Click the **Push to Git** option.

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Enter Commit Message

Provide a commit message describing what you’re pushing.

4

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Push

Click **Push** to send the selected items to Git.

![Push to Git Dialog](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg/resources/screenshots/push-flows-to-git-1.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg&q=85&s=4a8d86ac88f19fd22950fca77304226b) ![Push to Git Dialog](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg/resources/screenshots/push-flows-to-git-2.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg&q=85&s=91eddf7b759457b51720a3123dbb0dec)

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#rolling-back-a-release)

Rolling Back a Release
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If something goes wrong after applying a release, you can easily rollback to a previous state.

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Find the Release

Locate the release you want to rollback to in the releases list.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Click Rollback

Click the rollback icon (↩) next to the release.

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Review Changes

Review the changes that will be applied to restore that release state.

4

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#)

Apply Rollback

Select the changes to include and click **Apply Changes**.

![Rollback Release](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg/resources/screenshots/rollback-release.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg&q=85&s=83adc856e4f067ddaf32733313001ccb)

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#release-details)

Release Details
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each release in the list shows:

| Column | Description |
| --- | --- |
| **Name** | The name you gave the release |
| **Source** | Where the release came from (Git, Project, or Rollback) |
| **Imported At** | When the release was created |
| **Imported By** | The user who created the release |

Click on any release to view its full details. ![Release Details](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg/resources/screenshots/release-details.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=HfEX6NmvKT3DcQHg&q=85&s=4ea39e90eac163d569b7d18623fc7213)

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#understanding-the-changes-preview)

Understanding the Changes Preview
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When creating a release, you’ll see a preview of all changes:

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#flow-changes)

Flow Changes

*   New flows that will be created
*   Existing flows that will be updated
*   Flows that will be deleted

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#connection-changes)

Connection Changes

*   New connections are placeholders and must be reconnected after the release
*   Renamed connections

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#table-changes)

Table Changes

*   New, updated, and deleted tables are shown with their respective indicators

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#best-practices)

Best Practices
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Use Descriptive Names
---------------------

Give your releases meaningful names like “v1.2.0 - Added email notifications” to easily identify them later.

Review Before Applying
----------------------

Always review the changes preview carefully before applying a release to avoid unexpected modifications.

Test in Development
-------------------

If using Git sync, test changes in a development project before deploying to production.

Document Changes
----------------

Use the description field to document what changed and why for future reference.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#permissions)

Permissions
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To create and manage releases, you need the **Write Project Release** permission. Contact your instance administrator if you don’t have access to the releases feature.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases#troubleshooting)

Troubleshooting
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Environment settings are locked

The Environments feature must be enabled on your instance plan to use Git sync. Contact your instance administrator to upgrade your plan or enable this feature.

Git connection fails

*   Verify your SSH private key is correctly formatted (ends with an endline), and make sure it has an empty phrase.
*   Ensure the remote URL is in SSH format (not HTTPS)
*   Check that the branch exists in the repository

No changes detected

If no changes appear when creating a release, it means your current project is already in sync with the source.

Connection placeholders

After applying a release with new connections, navigate to the Connections page and reconnect them with valid credentials.

Push Everything button not visible

Make sure you configured your git settings and if you are selecting flows, make sure they are published.

Cannot find Environment settings

Navigate to **Project Settings** from the sidebar, then click on **Environment**. If you don’t see this option, the Environments feature may not be enabled for your instance.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/project-releases)

[Event Streaming](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/event-streaming)
[Security & Data Practices](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/practices)

⌘I

# AWS Secrets Manager - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Secret Managers

AWS Secrets Manager

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Prerequisites](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws#prerequisites)
    
*   [Step 1 — Create an IAM policy for Secrets Manager access](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws#step-1-%E2%80%94-create-an-iam-policy-for-secrets-manager-access)
    
*   [Step 2 — Create an IAM user and attach the policy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws#step-2-%E2%80%94-create-an-iam-user-and-attach-the-policy)
    
*   [Step 3 — Connect in Activepieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws#step-3-%E2%80%94-connect-in-activepieces)
    
*   [Using AWS Secrets Manager in connections](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws#using-aws-secrets-manager-in-connections)
    

AWS Secrets Manager helps you protect access to your applications, services, and IT resources. This integration uses **IAM user credentials** (Access Key + Secret Key) to authenticate directly with AWS Secrets Manager.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   An AWS account with permissions to create IAM users and policies
*   Permissions to create and manage secrets in AWS Secrets Manager

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws#step-1-%E2%80%94-create-an-iam-policy-for-secrets-manager-access)

Step 1 — Create an IAM policy for Secrets Manager access
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create an IAM policy that grants read access to the secrets Activepieces will retrieve.

1.  Open the [IAM console → Policies → Create policy](https://console.aws.amazon.com/iam/home#/policies$new?step=edit)
    .
2.  Switch to the **JSON** tab and paste:

    {
      "Version": "2012-10-17",
      "Statement": [\
        {\
          "Effect": "Allow",\
          "Action": [\
            "secretsmanager:GetSecretValue",\
            "secretsmanager:ListSecrets",\
            "secretsmanager:DescribeSecret"\
          ],\
          "Resource": "*"\
        }\
      ]
    }
    

For production, scope `Resource` to the specific secret ARNs Activepieces needs instead of using `"*"`.

3.  Click **Next**, name the policy (e.g. `ActivepiecesSecretsReadOnly`), and create it.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws#step-2-%E2%80%94-create-an-iam-user-and-attach-the-policy)

Step 2 — Create an IAM user and attach the policy
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Open the [IAM console → Users → Create user](https://console.aws.amazon.com/iam/home#/users$new)
    .
2.  Enter a username (e.g. `activepieces-secrets-user`) and click **Next**.
3.  Select **Attach policies directly**, find and attach the policy created in Step 1, then click **Next** and **Create user**.
4.  Open the newly created user, go to the **Security credentials** tab, and click **Create access key**.
5.  Select **Application running outside AWS**, click **Next**, then **Create access key**.
6.  Copy the **Access Key** and **Secret Key** — you will need both in the next step.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws#step-3-%E2%80%94-connect-in-activepieces)

Step 3 — Connect in Activepieces
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to **Platform Admin → Security → Secret Managers**.
2.  Select **AWS Secrets Manager** from the provider list.
3.  Enter the connection details:
    *   **Access Key** — the Access Key ID from Step 2 (e.g. `AKIAIOSFODNN7EXAMPLE`).
    *   **Secret Key** — the Secret Access Key from Step 2.
    *   **Region** — the AWS region where your secrets are stored (e.g. `us-east-1`).
4.  Click **Connect** to test and save the connection.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws#using-aws-secrets-manager-in-connections)

Using AWS Secrets Manager in connections
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When configuring a global connection that requires credentials:

1.  Click the **key icon** (🔑) next to the credential field.
2.  Select **AWS Secrets Manager** as the secret manager.
3.  Fill in:
    *   **Secret Name** — the friendly name of the secret in AWS Secrets Manager.
    *   **Secret Json key** — Key of row for the stored secret.

Activepieces will use the configured credentials to retrieve the secret value and inject it into the connection at runtime.

If you update existing secrets and you can’t see the update reflected . refer to [caching](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#caching)

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws)

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview)
[HashiCorp Vault](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/hashicorp)

⌘I

# HashiCorp Vault - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/hashicorp#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Secret Managers

HashiCorp Vault

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Prerequisites](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/hashicorp#prerequisites)
    
*   [Policies](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/hashicorp#policies)
    
*   [Connecting to Activepieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/hashicorp#connecting-to-activepieces)
    
*   [Using HashiCorp Vault Secrets](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/hashicorp#using-hashicorp-vault-secrets)
    

HashiCorp Vault is an enterprise-grade secrets management system that provides secure storage and access to secrets, API keys, passwords, and other sensitive data.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/hashicorp#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before connecting HashiCorp Vault to Activepieces, ensure you have:

*   **HashiCorp Vault Key-value (KV) secrets engine** version 2
*   **AppRole auth method** [enabled](https://developer.hashicorp.com/vault/docs/auth/approle)
    
*   **One or more AppRoles** [configured](https://developer.hashicorp.com/vault/docs/auth/approle)
     with appropriate policies

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/hashicorp#policies)

Policies
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enable The created AppRole to access your secrets engine(s) by adding the following to your policy

    path "sys/mounts" {
      capabilities = [ "read" ]
    }
    
    path "<secret_engine_name>/data/<secret_name>" {
      capabilities = [ "read" ]
    }
    

or

    path "sys/mounts" {
      capabilities = [ "read" ]
    }
    
    path "<secret_engine_name>/data/*" {
      capabilities = [ "read" ]
    }
    

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/hashicorp#connecting-to-activepieces)

Connecting to Activepieces
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to **Platform Admin → Security → Secret Managers**
2.  Click **New Connection** and select **HashiCorp Vault**
3.  Enter a **Name** for the connection
4.  Choose a **Scope** — **Platform** to make it available to all projects, or **Project** to restrict it to specific projects
5.  Fill in the connection details:
    *   **URL**: Your Vault server URL (e.g., `http://localhost:8200`)
    *   **Role ID**: The Role ID from your AppRole configuration
    *   **Secret ID**: The Secret ID from your AppRole configuration
    *   **Namespace** (optional): Vault namespace if using Vault Enterprise namespaces
6.  Click **Save** to test and save the connection

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/hashicorp#using-hashicorp-vault-secrets)

Using HashiCorp Vault Secrets
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once the connection is saved, you can reference Vault secrets inside any piece connection dialog — in global connections (Platform Admin) or directly in the flow builder.

1.  Open a connection dialog and click the **key icon** (🔑) next to a credential field
2.  Select your HashiCorp Vault connection from the dropdown
3.  Enter the secret path in the format: `mount/data/path/to/secret/key`

For example, if you stored a secret with:

    vault kv put -mount=secret mysec api_key='supersecret'
    

The path to enter would be:

    secret/data/mysec/api_key
    

![Manage Oauth2 apps](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/yqMjtHswhi3w4D2R/resources/screenshots/secret-manager.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=yqMjtHswhi3w4D2R&q=85&s=608015daeff79c8368a12c5fa2d488e0) The connection will automatically retrieve the secret from Vault when the flow runs.

If you update a secret in Vault and the change isn’t reflected in your flows, the cached value may still be active. Use the **refresh icon** next to the connection in the Secret Managers page to clear its cache immediately, or wait up to 1 hour for it to expire automatically. See [Caching](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#caching)
 for details.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/hashicorp.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/hashicorp)

[AWS Secrets Manager](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/aws)
[CyberArk Conjur](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur)

# How to Structure Projects - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Guides

How to Structure Projects

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

This feature is available in our paid editions. Contact us [here](https://www.activepieces.com/sales)
, and we'll be delighted to assist you!

Projects in Activepieces are the main units for organizing your automations and resources within your organization. Every project contains its own flows, connections, and tables. Access to these resources is shared among everyone who has access to that project. There are two types of projects:

*   **Personal Projects**: Each user invited to your organization automatically receives a personal project. This is a private space where only that user can create and manage flows, connections, and tables.
*   **Team Projects**: Team projects are shared spaces that can be created and managed from this page. Multiple users can be invited to a team project, allowing them to collaborate, share access to flows, connections, and tables, and work together.

When organizing your work, create team projects for group collaboration and utilize personal projects for individual or private tasks.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)

[How to Manage Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/manage-pieces)

# CyberArk Conjur - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Secret Managers

CyberArk Conjur

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Prerequisites](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#prerequisites)
    
*   [Conjur host configuration for Activepieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#conjur-host-configuration-for-activepieces)
    
*   [Example policy (Activepieces)](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#example-policy-activepieces)
    
*   [Policy steps (summary)](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#policy-steps-summary)
    
*   [Server URL and organization](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#server-url-and-organization)
    
*   [Connecting to Activepieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#connecting-to-activepieces)
    
*   [Using CyberArk Conjur secrets in connections](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#using-cyberark-conjur-secrets-in-connections)
    

CyberArk Conjur is a secrets management solution that provides secure storage and access to credentials. Integration with Activepieces uses **host/API key authentication**: Activepieces authenticates as a Conjur host, receives a short-lived token, and uses it to retrieve secrets for which that host has `read` and `execute` permissions. Conjur policies are defined in `.yml` files. For recommended structure and patterns, see [Policy best practices](https://docs.cyberark.com/conjur-enterprise/13.0/en/Content/Operations/Policy/policy-best-practices.htm)
 in the CyberArk Conjur documentation. For policy syntax and operators, see the [Policy syntax](https://docs.cyberark.com/conjur-open-source/Latest/en/Content/Operations/Policy/policy-syntax.htm)
 reference.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   A Conjur server (Conjur Cloud, Conjur Enterprise, or Conjur Open Source)
*   A Conjur policy that defines a host for Activepieces and grants it access to the variables you want to use

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#conjur-host-configuration-for-activepieces)

Conjur host configuration for Activepieces
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To allow Activepieces to read secrets, configure a Conjur policy that declares a group, variables, a host, a layer, and the right permissions. The steps below describe how to create that policy file.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#example-policy-activepieces)

Example policy (Activepieces)

The following policy defines a policy `activepieces` with a group, two variables, a host, a layer, and the grants so the host can read the variables.

    - !policy
      id: activepieces
      body:
        - !group activepieces-secrets
        - &variables
            - !variable
                id: key-1
                kind: password
            - !variable
                id: key-2
                kind: password
        - !permit
            role: !group /activepieces/activepieces-secrets
            privileges: [read, update, execute]
            resources: *variables
    
        - !host activepieces
        - !layer activepieces
        - !grant
            role: !layer activepieces
            members:
                - !host activepieces
        - !grant
            role: !group activepieces-secrets
            member: !layer activepieces
    

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#policy-steps-summary)

Policy steps (summary)

1.  **Declare a group** at the root of the policy (e.g. `activepieces-secrets`). This group will be allowed to read (and optionally execute) the variables.
2.  **Declare variables** and give the group `read` and `execute` on them (so the host can fetch secret values):
    
        - &variables
          - !variable
              id: my-secret
              kind: password
        - !permit
            role: !group /your-policy/your-group
            privileges: [read, execute]
            resources: *variables
        
    
3.  **Declare the host** that Activepieces will use (e.g. `activepieces`) and a **layer** (e.g. `activepieces`), and add the host to the layer:
    
        - !host activepieces
        - !layer activepieces
        - !grant
            role: !layer activepieces
            members:
                - !host activepieces
        
    
4.  **Grant the layer membership in the group** that has access to the variables:
    
        - !grant
          role: !group activepieces-secrets
          member: !layer activepieces
        
    
5.  **Load the policy** into Conjur. Conjur will create the host and return an **API key** for that host. You will use this API key and the host identity when connecting Activepieces.

After loading the policy, Conjur returns something like:

    {
      "created_roles": {
        "conjur:host:activepieces/activepieces": {
          "id": "conjur:host:activepieces/activepieces",
          "api_key": "<your-host-api-key>"
        }
      },
      "version": 1
    }
    

Store the **api\_key** securely; you will enter it in Activepieces as the **API Key**.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#server-url-and-organization)

Server URL and organization
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Conjur Cloud**: Use a URL of the form  
    `https://<subdomain>.secretsmgr.cyberark.cloud/api/`  
    and set **Organization account name** to `conjur` unless your Cloud tenant uses a different account.
*   **On-prem / Enterprise**: Use your Conjur server base URL (e.g. `https://conjur.example.com`) and your organization account name.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#connecting-to-activepieces)

Connecting to Activepieces
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to **Platform Admin → Security → Secret Managers**.
2.  Select **CyberArk Conjur** from the provider list.
3.  Enter the connection details:
    *   **URL**: Conjur server URL (e.g. `https://conjur.example.com` or Conjur Cloud URL above). Do not add a trailing slash.
    *   **Organization account name**: Your Conjur account (e.g. `conjur` for Conjur Cloud).
    *   **Login ID**: For host authentication this must be the Conjur host ID with a `host/` prefix, e.g. `host/activepieces/activepieces` (policy id and host name as in your policy).
    *   **API Key**: The host API key returned when the host was created (see policy load response above).
4.  Click **Connect** to test and save the connection.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur#using-cyberark-conjur-secrets-in-connections)

Using CyberArk Conjur secrets in connections
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When configuring a connection that uses a secret:

1.  Click the **key icon** (🔑) next to the credential field.
2.  Select a **CyberArk Conjur** connection from the list.
3.  Enter the **Secret key**: the Conjur variable path in the form `policy_id/variable_id`.  
    For the example policy above, use:
    *   `activepieces/key-1`
    *   `activepieces/key-2`

Activepieces will authenticate as the configured host and retrieve the secret from Conjur when the flow runs.

If you update existing secrets and you can’t see the update reflected . refer to [caching](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#caching)

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur)

[HashiCorp Vault](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/hashicorp)
[1Password](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword)

⌘I

# 1Password - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Secret Managers

1Password

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Prerequisites](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword#prerequisites)
    
*   [Step 1 — Create a service account](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword#step-1-%E2%80%94-create-a-service-account)
    
*   [Step 2 — Connect in Activepieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword#step-2-%E2%80%94-connect-in-activepieces)
    
*   [Using 1Password in connections](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword#using-1password-in-connections)
    
*   [Example secret references](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword#example-secret-references)
    

1Password Secrets Automation lets you securely store and retrieve credentials from 1Password vaults. This integration uses a **service account token** to authenticate with the 1Password SDK.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   A 1Password account with the **Teams** or **Business** plan (service accounts require a paid plan)
*   Permission to create service accounts in your 1Password account

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword#step-1-%E2%80%94-create-a-service-account)

Step 1 — Create a service account
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Sign in to [1password.com](https://1password.com/)
     and go to **Developer Tools → Service Accounts**.
2.  Click **Create a service account**.
3.  Give it a name (e.g. `Activepieces`).
4.  Grant it **Read Items** access on the vaults Activepieces needs to access.
5.  Click **Create service account** and copy the token — it starts with `ops_` and is shown only once.

Store the token securely. Once you leave the page, 1Password will not show it again.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword#step-2-%E2%80%94-connect-in-activepieces)

Step 2 — Connect in Activepieces
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to **Platform Admin → Security → Secret Managers**.
2.  Select **1Password** from the provider list.
3.  Paste the **Service Account Token** from Step 1.
4.  Click **Connect** to test and save the connection.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword#using-1password-in-connections)

Using 1Password in connections
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When configuring a global connection that requires credentials:

1.  Click the **key icon** (🔑) next to the credential field.
2.  Select a **1Password** connection from the list.
3.  Enter the **Secret Reference** in the format:
    
        op://vault/item/field
        
    
    *   **vault** — the vault name or ID (e.g. `Production`)
    *   **item** — the item title or ID (e.g. `Stripe`)
    *   **field** — the field label within the item (e.g. `password`, `api key`)

Activepieces will retrieve the secret value from 1Password and inject it into the connection at runtime.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword#example-secret-references)

Example secret references
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| 1Password location | Reference |
| --- | --- |
| Vault `Production` → Item `Stripe` → Field `Secret Key` | `op://Production/Stripe/Secret Key` |
| Vault `Shared` → Item `Database` → Field `password` | `op://Shared/Database/password` |

If you update existing secrets and you can’t see the update reflected, refer to [caching](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/overview#caching)
.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/onepassword)

[CyberArk Conjur](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/secret-managers/cyberark-conjur)
[Manage User Roles](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/permissions)

⌘I

# Security & Data Practices - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/practices#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Security

Security & Data Practices

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [External Systems Credentials](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/practices#external-systems-credentials)
    
*   [Vulnerability Disclosure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/practices#vulnerability-disclosure)
    
*   [Access and Authentication](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/practices#access-and-authentication)
    
*   [Privacy & Data](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/practices#privacy-%26-data)
    

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/practices#external-systems-credentials)

External Systems Credentials
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Storing Credentials** All credentials are stored with 256-bit encryption keys, and there is no API to retrieve them for the user. They are sent only during processing, after which access is revoked from the engine. **Data Masking** We implement a robust data masking mechanism where third-party credentials or any sensitive information are systematically censored within the logs, guaranteeing that sensitive information is never stored or documented. **OAuth2** Integrations with third parties are always done using OAuth2, with a limited number of scopes when third-party support allows.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/practices#vulnerability-disclosure)

Vulnerability Disclosure
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Activepieces is an open-source project that welcomes contributors to test and report security issues. For detailed information about our security policy, please refer to our GitHub Security Policy at: [https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/security/policy](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/security/policy)

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/practices#access-and-authentication)

Access and Authentication
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Role-Based Access Control (RBAC)** To manage user access, we utilize Role-Based Access Control (RBAC). Team admins assign roles to users, granting them specific permissions to access and interact with projects, folders, and resources. RBAC allows for fine-grained control, enabling administrators to define and enforce access policies based on user roles. **Single Sign-On (SSO)** Implementing Single Sign-On (SSO) serves as a pivotal component of our security strategy. SSO streamlines user authentication by allowing them to access Activepieces with a single set of credentials. This not only enhances user convenience but also strengthens security by reducing the potential attack surface associated with managing multiple login credentials. **Audit Logs** We maintain comprehensive audit logs to track and monitor all access activities within Activepieces. This includes user interactions, system changes, and other relevant events. Our meticulous logging helps identify security threats and ensures transparency and accountability in our security measures. **Password Policy Enforcement** Users log in to Activepieces using a password known only to them. Activepieces enforces password length and complexity standards. Passwords are not stored; instead, only a secure hash of the password is stored in the database. For more information.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/practices#privacy-&-data)

Privacy & Data
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Supported Cloud Regions** Presently, our cloud services are available in Germany as the supported data region. We have plans to expand to additional regions in the near future. If you opt for **self-hosting**, the available regions will depend on where you choose to host. **Policy** To better understand how we handle your data and prioritize your privacy, please take a moment to review our [Privacy Policy](https://www.activepieces.com/privacy)
. This document outlines in detail the measures we take to safeguard your information and the principles guiding our approach to privacy and data protection.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/admin-guide/security/practices.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/admin-guide/security/practices)

[Project Releases](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/project-releases)
[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/audit-logs/overview)

# Create/Update Connections - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-connections#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Misc

Create/Update Connections

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

**Requirements:**

*   Activepieces version 0.34.5 or higher
*   SDK version 0.3.2 or higher

If you would like your users to use your own OAuth2 apps, we recommend you check [this](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-console/manage-oauth2)
.

“connectionName” is the externalId of the connection (you can get it by hovering the connection name in the connections table).  
We kept the same parameter name for backward compatibility, anyone upgrading their instance from < 0.35.1, will not face issues in that regard.

**Breaking Change:**  
  
If your Activepieces instance version is < 0.45.0 and (you are using the connect method from the embed sdk, and need the connection externalId to be returned after the user creates it OR if you want to reconnect a specific connection with an externalId), you must upgrade your instance to >= 0.45.0

*   You can use the embedded SDK in your SaaS to allow your users to create connections and store them in Activepieces.

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-connections#)

Initialize the SDK

Follow the instructions in the [Embed Builder](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder)
.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-connections#)

Call Connect Method

After initializing the SDK, you will have access to a property called `activepieces` inside your `window` object. Call its `connect` method to open a new connection dialog as follows.

    <script> 
    activepieces.connect({pieceName:'@activepieces/piece-google-sheets'});
    </script>
    

**Connect Parameters:**

| Parameter Name | Required | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| pieceName | ✅   | string | The name of the piece you want to create a connection for. |
| connectionName | ❌   | string | The external Id of the connection (you can get it by hovering the connection name in the connections table), when provided the connection created/upserted will use this as the external Id and display name. |
| newWindow | ❌   | { width?: number, height?: number, top?: number, left?: number } | If set the connection dialog will be opened in a new window instead of an iframe taking the full page. |

**Connect Result**The `connect` method returns a `promise` that resolves to the following:

    {
        connection?: {
            id: string,
            name: string
        }
    }
    

`name` is the externalId of the connection. `connection` is undefined if the user closes the dialog and doesn’t create a connection.

You can use the `connections` piece in the builder to retrieve the created connection using its name.![Connections in Builder](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP/resources/screenshots/connections-piece.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP&q=85&s=78986f41685be71b8983da0980e56554)![Connections in Builder](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP/resources/screenshots/connections-piece-usage.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP&q=85&s=5f4f2ee7c3338ae41ac03ca8f734d8b7)

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/embedding/embed-connections.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/embedding/embed-connections)

[Show/Hide Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/customize-pieces)
[Navigation](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/navigation)

⌘I

# Overview - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Get Started

Overview

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Authentication:](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview#authentication)
    
*   [Pagination](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview#pagination)
    

API keys are generated under the platform dashboard at this moment to manage multiple projects, which is only available in the Platform and Enterprise editions, Please contact [\[email protected\]](https://www.activepieces.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#82f1e3eee7f1c2e3e1f6ebf4e7f2ebe7e1e7f1ace1edef)
 for more information.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview#authentication)

Authentication:

The API uses “API keys” to authenticate requests. You can view and manage your API keys from the Platform Dashboard. After creating your API key, you can pass the API key as a Bearer token in the header. Example: `Authorization: Bearer {API_KEY}`

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview#pagination)

Pagination

All endpoints use seek pagination, to paginate through the results, you can provide the `limit` and `cursor` as query parameters. The API response will have the following structure:

    {
        "data": [],
        "next": "string",
        "previous": "string"
    }
    

*   **`data`**: Holds the requested results or data.
*   **`next`**: Provides a starting cursor for the next set of results, if available.
*   **`previous`**: Provides a starting cursor for the previous set of results, if applicable.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/endpoints/overview.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/endpoints/overview)

[Project Schema](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/projects/schema)

# Overview - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Essentials

Overview

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

This feature is available in our paid editions. Contact us [here](https://www.activepieces.com/sales)
, and we'll be delighted to assist you!

This section provides an overview of how to embed the Activepieces builder in your application and automatically provision the user. The embedding process involves the following steps:

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview#)

Provision Users

Generate a JSON Web Token (JWT) to identify your customer and pass it to the SDK, read more [here](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/provision-users)
.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview#)

Embed Builder

You can use the SDK to embed and customize Activepieces in your SaaS, read more [here](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder)
.

Here is an example of how it looks like in one of the SaaS that embed Activepieces: ![Embedding Example](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/screenshots/embedding-example.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-&q=85&s=5c4ee73a251a6dc600344361ba8e0e3c)

In case, you need to gather connections from your users in your SaaS. You can do this with the SDK. Find more info [here](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-connections)
.

If you are looking for a way to communicate between Activpieces and the SaaS embedding it through a piece, we recommend you check the [custom property doc](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/properties#custom-property-beta)

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/embedding/overview.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/embedding/overview)

[Provision Users](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/provision-users)

# Show/Hide Pieces - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/customize-pieces#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Misc

Show/Hide Pieces

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

This feature is available in our paid editions. Contact us [here](https://www.activepieces.com/sales)
, and we'll be delighted to assist you!

If you would like your users to use your own OAuth2 apps, we recommend you check [this](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-console/manage-oauth2)
.

If you would like to only show specific pieces to your embedding users, we recommend you do the following:

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/customize-pieces#)

Tag Pieces

Tag the pieces you would like to show to your user by going to **Platform Admin -> Setup -> Pieces**, selecting the pieces you would like to tag and hit **Apply Tags**![Bulk Tag](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/screenshots/tag-pieces.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-&q=85&s=3a225095e3c85e8aaac53f6c0fad62ff)

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/customize-pieces#)

Add Tags to Provision Token

You need to specify the tags of pieces in the token, check how to generate token in [provisioning users](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/provision-users)
.You should specify the `pieces` claim like this:

    {
        /// Other claims
        "piecesFilterType": "ALLOWED",
        "piecesTags": [ "free" ]
    }
    

Each time the token is used by the embedding SDK, it will sync all pieces with these tags to the token’s project. The project will only contain the pieces that contain these tags.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/embedding/customize-pieces.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/embedding/customize-pieces)

[Embed Builder](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder)
[Create/Update Connections](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-connections)

⌘I

---

Git Sync

Git Repos Schema

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

Example

    {
      "id": "<string>",
      "created": "<string>",
      "updated": "<string>",
      "remoteUrl": "<string>",
      "branch": "<string>",
      "branchType": "PRODUCTION",

Add a piece to a platform

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://cloud.activepieces.com/api/v1/pieces \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "packageType": "ARCHIVE",
      "scope": "PLATFORM",
      "pieceName": "<string>",
      "pieceVersion": "<string>",
      "pieceArchive": {
        "filename": "<string>",
        "data": "<unknown>",
        "type": "file",
        "mimetype": "<string>"
      }
    }
    '

201

    {}

v1

/

pieces

Try it

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://cloud.activepieces.com/api/v1/pieces \

      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "packageType": "ARCHIVE",
      "scope": "PLATFORM",
      "pieceName": "<string>",
      "pieceVersion": "<string>",
      "pieceArchive": {
        "filename": "<string>",

# Predefined Connection - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/predefined-connection#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Misc

Predefined Connection

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Prerequisites](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/predefined-connection#prerequisites)
    
*   [Create a Predefined Connection](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/predefined-connection#create-a-predefined-connection)
    
*   [Hide the Connections Dropdown (Optional)](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/predefined-connection#hide-the-connections-dropdown-optional)
    

Use predefined connections to allow users to access your piece in the embedded app without re-entering authentication credentials. The high-level steps are:

*   Create a global connection for a project using the API in the platform admin. Only platform admins can edit or delete global connections.
*   (Optional) Hide the connections dropdown in the piece settings.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/predefined-connection#prerequisites)

Prerequisites

*   [Run the Enterprise Edition](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/run-ee)
    
*   [Create your piece](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
    . Later we will customize the piece logic to use predefined connections.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/predefined-connection#create-a-predefined-connection)

Create a Predefined Connection

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/predefined-connection#)

Create an API Key

Go to **Platform Admin → Security → API Keys** and create an API key. Save it for use in the next step.![Create API Key](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP/resources/screenshots/create-api-key.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP&q=85&s=423bb1176e0d1efdce61745c08be43e5)

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/predefined-connection#)

Create a Global Connection via API

Add the following snippet to your backend to create a global connection each time you generate the **JWT token**.The snippet does the following:

*   Create Project If it doesn’t exist.
*   Create a global connection for the project with certain naming convention.

    const apiKey = 'YOUR_API_KEY';
    const instanceUrl = 'https://cloud.activepieces.com';
    
    // The name of the user / organization in your SAAS
    const externalProjectId = 'org_1234';
    const pieceName = '@activepieces/piece-gelato';
    // This will depend on what your piece auth type is, can be one of this ['PLATFORM_OAUTH2','SECRET_TEXT','BASIC_AUTH','CUSTOM_AUTH']
    const pieceAuthType = "CUSTOM_AUTH"
    const connectionProps = {
        // Fill in the props required by your piece's auth
    }
    const { id: projectId, externalId } = await getOrCreateProject({
      projectExternalId: externalProjectId,
      apiKey,
      instanceUrl,
    });
    
    await createGlobalConnection({
      projectId,
      externalProjectId,
      apiKey,
      instanceUrl,
      pieceName,
      props,
      pieceAuthType
    });
    
    

Implementation:

    async function getOrCreateProject({
        projectExternalId,
        apiKey,
        instanceUrl,
    }: {
        projectExternalId: string,
        apiKey: string,
        instanceUrl: string
    }): Promise<{ id: string, externalId: string }> {
    
        const projects = await fetch(`${instanceUrl}/api/v1/projects?externalId=${projectExternalId}`, {
            method: 'GET',
            headers: {
                'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
                'Content-Type': 'application/json'
            },
        })
            .then(response => response.json())
            .then(data => data.data)
            .catch(err => {
                console.error('Error fetching projects:', err);
                return [];
            });
    
        if (projects.length > 0) {
            return {
                id: projects[0].id,
                externalId: projects[0].externalId
            };
        }
    
        const newProject = await fetch(`${instanceUrl}/api/v1/projects`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
                'Content-Type': 'application/json'
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                displayName: projectExternalId,
                metadata: {},
                externalId: projectExternalId
            })
        })
            .then(response => response.json())
            .catch(err => {
                console.error('Error creating project:', err);
                throw err;
            });
    
        return {
            id: newProject.id,
            externalId: newProject.externalId
        };
    } 
    
    async function createGlobalConnection({
        projectId,
        externalProjectId,
        apiKey,
        instanceUrl,
        pieceName,
        props,
        pieceAuthType
    }: {
        projectId: string,
        externalProjectId: string,
        apiKey: string,
        instanceUrl: string,
        pieceName: string,
        props: Record<string, any>,
        pieceAuthType
    }) {
    
        const displayName = 'Gelato Connection';
        const connectionExternalId = 'gelato_' + externalProjectId;
    
        return fetch(`${instanceUrl}/api/v1/global-connections`, {
            method: 'POST',
            headers: {
                'Authorization': `Bearer ${apiKey}`,
                'Content-Type': 'application/json'
            },
            body: JSON.stringify({
                displayName,
                pieceName,
                metadata: {},
                type: pieceAuthType,
                value: {
                    type: pieceAuthType,
                    props
                },
                scope: 'PLATFORM',
                projectIds: [projectId],
                externalId: connectionExternalId
            })
        });
    }
    

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/predefined-connection#hide-the-connections-dropdown-optional)

Hide the Connections Dropdown (Optional)

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/predefined-connection#)

Modify Trigger / Action Definition

Wherever you call `createTrigger` or `createAction` set `requireAuth` to `false`, this will hide the connections dropdown in the piece settings in the builder, next we need to fetch it based on a naming convention.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/predefined-connection#)

Fetch the connection

Here is example how you can fetch the connection value based on naming convention, make sure this naming convention is followed when creating a global connection.

    import {
       ConnectionsManager,
       Property,
       TriggerStrategy
    } from "@activepieces/pieces-framework";
    import {
       createTrigger
    } from "@activepieces/pieces-framework";
    import {
       isNil
    } from "@activepieces/shared";
    // Add this import from the index.ts file, where it contains the definition of the auth object.
    import { auth } from '../..';
    
    const fetchConnection = async (
    	connections: ConnectionsManager,
    	projectExternalId: string | undefined,
    ): Promise<PiecePropValueSchema<typeof auth>> => {
    	if (isNil(projectExternalId)) {
    		throw new Error('This project is missing an external id');
    	}
    	// the naming convention here is gelato_projectExternalId
    	const connection = await connections.get(`gelato_${projectExternalId}`);
    	if (isNil(connection)) {
    		throw new Error(`Connection not found for project ${projectExternalId}`);
    	}
    
    	return connection as PiecePropValueSchema<typeof auth>;
    };
    
    
    export const newFlavorCreated = createTrigger({
       requireAuth: false,
       name: 'newFlavorCreated',
       displayName: 'new flavor created',
       description: 'triggers when a new icecream flavor is created.',
       props: {
          dropdown: Property.Dropdown({
             displayName: 'Dropdown',
             required: true,
             refreshers: [],
             options: async (_, {
                connections,
                project
             }) => {
                const connection = await fetchConnection(connections, (await project.externalId()));
                // your logic
                return {
                   options: [{\
                      label: 'test',\
                      value: 'test'\
                   }]
                }
             }
          })
       },
       sampleData: {},
       type: TriggerStrategy.POLLING,
       async test({connections,project}) {
          const connection = await fetchConnection(connections, (await project.externalId()));
          // use the connection with your own logic
          return []
       },
       async onEnable({connections,project}) {
          const connection = await fetchConnection(connections, (await project.externalId()));
          // use the connection with your own logic
       },
    
       async onDisable({connections,project}) {
          const connection = await fetchConnection(connections, (await project.externalId()));
          // use the connection with your own logic
       },
    
       async run({connections,project}) {
        const connection = await fetchConnection(connections, (await project.externalId()));
          // use the connection with your own logic
          return []
       },
    });
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/embedding/predefined-connection.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/embedding/predefined-connection)

Project Releases

Project Release Schema

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

Example

    {
      "id": "<string>",
      "created": "<string>",
      "updated": "<string>",
      "projectId": "<string>",
      "name": "<string>",
      "fileId": "<string>",
      "type": "GIT",
      "description": "<string>",
      "importedBy": "<string>"
    }

# API Requests - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-server-requests#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Misc

API Requests

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

**Requirements:**

*   Activepieces version 0.34.5 or higher
*   SDK version 0.3.6 or higher

You can use the embedded SDK to send requests to your instance and retrieve data.

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-server-requests#)

Initialize the SDK

Follow the instructions in the [Embed Builder](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder)
 to initialize the SDK.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-server-requests#)

Call (request) Method

    <script> 
    activepieces.request({path:'/flows',method:'GET'}).then(console.log);
    </script>
    

**Request Parameters:**

| Parameter Name | Required | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| path | ✅   | string | The path within your instance you want to hit (we prepend the path with your\_instance\_url/api/v1) |
| method | ✅   | string | The http method to use ‘GET’, ‘POST’,‘PUT’, ‘DELETE’, ‘OPTIONS’, ‘PATCH’ and ‘HEAD |
| body | ❌   | JSON object | The json body of your request |
| queryParams | ❌   | Record<string,string> | The query params to include in your request |

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/embedding/sdk-server-requests.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/embedding/sdk-server-requests)

[SDK Changelog](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog)

⌘I

cURL

    curl --request GET \
      --url https://cloud.activepieces.com/api/v1/flow-runs \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>'

200

    {
      "data": [\
        {\
          "id": "<string>",\
