#### Authorizations

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#authorization-authorization)

Authorization

string

header

required

Use your api key generated from the admin console

#### Query Parameters

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#parameter-flow-id)

flowId

string\[\]

Pattern: `^[0-9a-zA-Z]{21}$`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#parameter-tags)

tags

string\[\]

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#parameter-status)

status

enum<string>\[\]

Available options:

`FAILED`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#parameter-limit)

limit

number

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#parameter-cursor)

cursor

string

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#parameter-created-after)

createdAfter

string

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#parameter-created-before)

createdBefore

string

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#parameter-project-id)

projectId

string

required

Pattern: `^[0-9a-zA-Z]{21}$`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#parameter-failed-step-name)

failedStepName

string

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#parameter-flow-run-ids)

flowRunIds

string\[\]

Pattern: `^[0-9a-zA-Z]{21}$`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#parameter-include-archived)

includeArchived

boolean

#### Response

200 - application/json

Default Response

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#response-data)

data

object\[\]

required

Show child attributes

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#response-next-one-of-0)

next

string | null

Cursor to the next page

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/flow-runs/list#response-previous-one-of-0)

previous

string | null

Cursor to the previous page

# Overview - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Build a Piece

Overview

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

Building pieces is fun and important; it allows you to customize Activepieces for your own needs.

We love contributions! In fact, most of the pieces are contributed by the community. Feel free to open a pull request.

**Friendly Tip:** For the fastest support, we recommend joining our Discord community. We are dedicated to addressing every question and concern raised there.

Code with TypeScript
--------------------

Build pieces using TypeScript for a more powerful and flexible development process.

Hot Reloading
-------------

See your changes in the browser within 7 seconds.

Open Source
-----------

Work within the open-source environment, explore, and contribute to other pieces.

Community Support
-----------------

Join our large community, where you can ask questions, share ideas, and develop alongside others.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)

[Start Building](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/start-building)

⌘I

---

Audit Logs

Signing Key Created

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

Example

    {
      "id": "<string>",
      "created": "<string>",
      "updated": "<string>",
      "platformId": "<string>",
      "action": "signing.key.created",
      "data": {
        "signingKey": {
          "id": "<string>",
          "created": "<string>",
          "updated": "<string>",
          "displayName": "<string>"
        }
      },
      "projectId": "<string>",
      "projectDisplayName": "<string>",
      "userId": "<string>",
      "userEmail": "<string>",
      "ip": "<string>"
    }

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/audit-logs/signing-key-created#schema-id)

id

string

required

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/audit-logs/signing-key-created#schema-created)

created

string

required

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/audit-logs/signing-key-created#schema-updated)

updated

string

required

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/audit-logs/signing-key-created#schema-platform-id)

platformId

string

required

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/audit-logs/signing-key-created#schema-action)

action

enum<string>

required

Available options:

`signing.key.created`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/audit-logs/signing-key-created#schema-data)

data

object

required

Show child attributes

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/audit-logs/signing-key-created#schema-project-id)

projectId

string

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/audit-logs/signing-key-created#schema-project-display-name)

projectDisplayName

string

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/audit-logs/signing-key-created#schema-user-id)

userId

string

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/audit-logs/signing-key-created#schema-user-email)

userEmail

string

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/security/audit-logs/signing-key-created#schema-ip)

ip

string

*   [04/12/2024 (0.3.0)](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#04%2F12%2F2024-0-3-0)
    

**Breaking Change:**  
  
If your Activepieces image version is < 0.45.0 and (you are using the connect method from the embed SDk, and need the connection externalId to be returned after the user creates it OR if you want to reconnect a specific connection with an externalId), you must upgrade your Activepieces image to >= 0.45.0

Between Acitvepieces image version 0.32.1 and 0.46.4 the navigation handler was including the project id in the path, this might have broken implementation logic for people using the navigation handler, this has been fixed from 0.46.5 and onwards, the handler won’t show the project id prepended to routes.

Change log format: MM/DD/YYYY (version)

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#10/27/2025-0-8-1)

10/27/2025 (0.8.1)

*   SDK URL: [https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.8.1.js](https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.8.1.js)
    
*   Fixed a bug where if you didn’t start your navigation route with ’/’ it would redirect you to ‘/flows’

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#09/21/2025-0-8-0)

09/21/2025 (0.8.0)

*   SDK URL: [https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.8.0.js](https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.8.0.js)
    
*   This version requires you to **upgrade Activepieces to [0.70.0](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/releases/tag/0.70.0)
    **.
*   Removed `embedding.dashboard.hideSettings`.
*   Added `embedding.dashboard.hidePageHeader` parameter to the [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method **(value: true | false)**.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#07/30/2025-0-7-0)

07/30/2025 (0.7.0)

*   SDK URL: [https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.7.0.js](https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.7.0.js)
    
*   This version requires you to **upgrade Activepieces to [0.66.7](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/releases/tag/0.66.7)
    **
*   Added `embedding.dashboard.hideSettings` parameter to the [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method **(value: true | false)**.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#07/07/2025-0-6-0)

07/07/2025 (0.6.0)

*   SDK URL: [https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.6.0.js](https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.6.0.js)
    
*   This version requires you to **upgrade Activepieces to [0.66.1](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/releases/tag/0.66.1)
    **
*   Added `embedding.dashboard.hideFlowsPageNavbar` parameter to the [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method **(value: true | false)**.
*   **(Breaking Change)** `embedding.dashboard.hideSidebar` used to hide the navbar above the flows table in the dashboard now it relies on `embedding.dashboard.hideFlowsPageNavbar`.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#03/07/2025-0-5-0)

03/07/2025 (0.5.0)

*   SDK URL: [https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.5.0.js](https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.5.0.js)
    
*   This version requires you to **upgrade Activepieces to [0.64.2](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/releases/tag/0.64.2)
    **
*   Added `embedding.hideDuplicateFlow` parameter to the [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method **(value: true | false)**.
*   Added `embedding.builder.homeButtonIcon` parameter to the [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method **(value: ‘logo’ | ‘back’)**, if set to **‘back’** the tooltip shown on hovering the home button is removed.
*   Added `embedding.locale` parameter to the [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method, it takes [ISO 639-1](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_ISO_639_language_codes)
     locale codes, here are the ones supported: **(‘en’ | ‘nl’ | ‘it’ | ‘de’ | ‘fr’ | ‘bg’ | ‘uk’ | ‘hu’ | ‘es’ | ‘ja’ | ‘id’ | ‘vi’ | ‘zh’ | ‘pt’)**
*   Added `embedding.styling.mode` parameter to [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method **(value: ‘light’ | ‘dark’)**
*   **(Breaking Change)** Removed `embedding.builder.hideLogo` parameter from the [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method.
*   **(Breaking Change)** Removed MCP methods from sdk.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#17/06/2025-0-5-0-rc-1)

17/06/2025 (0.5.0-rc.1)

*   SDK URL: [https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.5.0-rc.1.js](https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.5.0-rc.1.js)
    
*   This version requires you to **upgrade Activepieces to [0.64.0-rc.0](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/pkgs/container/activepieces/438888138?tag=0.64.0-rc.0)
    **
*   Revert back the `prefix` parameter from the [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#16/06/2025-0-5-0-rc-0)

16/06/2025 (0.5.0-rc.0)

*   SDK URL: [https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.5.0-rc.0.js](https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.5.0-rc.0.js)
    
*   This version requires you to **upgrade Activepieces to [0.64.0-rc.0](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/pkgs/container/activepieces/438888138?tag=0.64.0-rc.0)
    **
*   Added `embedding.hideDuplicateFlow` parameter to the [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method **(value: true | false)**.
*   Added `embedding.builder.homeButtonIcon` parameter to the [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method **(value: ‘logo’ | ‘back’)**, if set to **‘back’** the tooltip shown on hovering the home button is removed.
*   Added `embedding.locale` parameter to the [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method, it takes [ISO 639-1](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_ISO_639_language_codes)
     locale codes, here are the ones supported: **(‘en’ | ‘nl’ | ‘it’ | ‘de’ | ‘fr’ | ‘bg’ | ‘uk’ | ‘hu’ | ‘es’ | ‘ja’ | ‘id’ | ‘vi’ | ‘zh’ | ‘pt’)**
*   Added `embedding.styling.mode` parameter to [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method **(value: ‘light’ | ‘dark’)**
*   **(Breaking Change)** Removed `prefix` parameter from the [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method.
*   **(Breaking Change)** Removed `embedding.builder.hideLogo` parameter from the [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#26/05/2025-0-4-1)

26/05/2025 (0.4.1)

*   Fixed an issue where sometimes the embed HTML file was getting cached.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#20/05/2025-0-4-0)

20/05/2025 (0.4.0)

— Note: we didn’t consider adding optional new parameters as a breaking change so we were bumping the patch version, but that was wrong and we will begin bumping the minor version for those changes from now on, and patch version will only get bumped for bug fixes.

*   This version requires you to update Activepieces to 0.56.0
*   Added `embedding.hideExportAndImportFlow` parameter to the [configure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-parameters)
     method.
*   Added new possible value to the configure method param `embed.builder.disableNavigation` which is “keep\_home\_button\_only” that keeps only the home button and hides the folder name with the delete flow action.
*   Added new param to the configure method `embed.builder.homeButtonClickedHandler`, that overrides the navigation behaviour on clicking the home button.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#17/04/2025-0-3-7)

17/04/2025 (0.3.7)

*   Added MCP methods to update MCP configurations.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#16/04/2025-0-3-6)

16/04/2025 (0.3.6)

*   Added the [request](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-server-requests)
     method which allows you to call our backend API.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#24/2/2025-0-3-5)

24/2/2025 (0.3.5)

*   Added a new parameter to the connect method to make the connection dialog a popup instead of an iframe taking the full page.
*   Fixed a bug where the returned promise from the connect method was always resolved to {connection: undefined}
*   Now when you use the connect method with the “connectionName” parameter, the user will reconnect to the connection with the matching externalId instead of creating a new one.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#04/02/2025-0-3-4)

04/02/2025 (0.3.4)

*   This version requires you to update Activepieces to 0.41.0
*   Adds the ability to pass font family name and font url to the embed sdk

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#26/01/2025-0-3-3)

26/01/2025 (0.3.3)

*   This version requires you to update Activepieces to 0.39.8
*   activepieces.configure method was being resolved before the user was authenticated, this is fixed now, so you can use activepieces.navigate method to navigate to your desired initial route.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#04/12/2024-0-3-0)

04/12/2024 (0.3.0)

*   add custom navigation handler ([#4500](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/pull/4500)
    )
*   allow passing a predefined name for connection in connect method ([#4485](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/pull/4485)
    )

# Embed Builder - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Essentials

Embed Builder

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Configure SDK](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-sdk)
    

This feature is available in our paid editions. Contact us [here](https://www.activepieces.com/sales)
, and we'll be delighted to assist you!

This documentation explains how to embed the Activepieces iframe inside your application and customize it.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-builder#configure-sdk)

Configure SDK
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Adding the embedding SDK script will initialize an object in your window called `activepieces`, which has a method called `configure` that you should call after the container has been rendered.

The following scripts shouldn’t contain the `async` or `defer` attributes.

These steps assume you have already generated a JWT token from the backend. If not, please check the [provision-users](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/provision-users)
 page.

    <script src="https://cdn.activepieces.com/sdk/embed/0.8.1.js">
    </script>
    <script>
    const instanceUrl = 'YOUR_INSTANCE_URL';
    const jwtToken = 'GENERATED_JWT_TOKEN';
    const containerId = 'YOUR_CONTAINER_ID';
    activepieces.configure({
      instanceUrl,
      jwtToken,
      prefix: "/",
      embedding: {
        containerId,
        builder: {
          disableNavigation: false,
          hideFlowName: false
        },
        dashboard: {
          hideSidebar: false
        },
        hideFolders: false,
        navigation: {
          handler: ({ route }) => {
              // The iframe route has changed, make sure you check the navigation section.
            }
        }
      },
    });
    
    </script>
    

`configure` returns a promise which is resolved after authentication is done.

Please check the [navigation](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/navigation)
 section, as it’s very important to understand how navigation works and how to supply an auto-sync experience.

**Configure Parameters:**

| Parameter Name | Required | Type | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| instanceUrl | ✅   | string | The url of the instance hosting Activepieces, could be [https://cloud.activepieces.com](https://cloud.activepieces.com/)<br> if you are a cloud user. |
| jwtToken | ✅   | string | The jwt token you generated to authenticate your users to Activepieces. |
| prefix | ❌   | string | Some customers have an embedding prefix, like this `<embedding_url_prefix>/<Activepieces_url>`. For example if the prefix is `/automation` and the Activepieces url is `/flows` the full url would be `/automation/flows`. |
| embedding.containerId | ❌   | string | The html element’s id that is going to be containing Activepieces’s iframe. |
| embedding.builder.disableNavigation | ❌   | boolean \| `keep_home_button_only` | Hides the folder name, home button (if not set to [`keep_home_button_only`](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#20%2F05%2F2025-0-4-0)<br>) and delete option in the builder, by default it is false. |
| embedding.builder.hideFlowName | ❌   | boolean | Hides the flow name and flow actions dropdown in the builder’s header, by default it is false. |
| embedding.builder.homeButtonClickedHandler | ❌   | `()=>void` | Callback that stops home button from navigating to dashboard and overrides it with this handler (added in [0.4.0](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#20%2F05%2F2025-0-4-0)<br>) |
| embedding.builder.homeButtonIcon | ❌   | `logo` \| `back` | if set to **`back`** the tooltip shown on hovering the home button is removed (added in [0.5.0](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#03%2F07%2F2025-0-5-0)<br>) |
| embedding.dashboard.hideSidebar | ❌   | boolean | Controls the visibility of the sidebar in the dashboard, by default it is false. |
| embedding.dashboard.hideFlowsPageNavbar | ❌   | boolean | Controls the visibility of the navbar showing flows,issues and runs above the flows table in the dashboard, by default it is false. (added in [0.6.0](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#07%2F07%2F2025-0-6-0)<br>) |
| embedding.dashboard.hidePageHeader | ❌   | boolean | Hides the page header in the dashboard by default it is false. (added in [0.8.0](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#09%2F21%2F2025-0-8-0)<br>) |
| embedding.hideFolders | ❌   | boolean | Hides all things related to folders in both the flows table and builder by default it is false. |
| embedding.styling.fontUrl | ❌   | string | The url of the font to be used in the embedding, by default it is `https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Roboto:wght@300;400;500;700&display=swap`. |
| embedding.styling.fontFamily | ❌   | string | The font family to be used in the embedding, by default it is `Roboto`. |
| embedding.styling.mode | ❌   | `light` \| `dark` | Controls light/dark mode (added in [0.5.0](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#03%2F07%2F2025-0-5-0)<br>) |
| embedding.hideExportAndImportFlow | ❌   | boolean | Hides the option to export or import flows (added in [0.4.0](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#20%2F05%2F2025-0-4-0)<br>) |
| embedding.hideDuplicateFlow | ❌   | boolean | Hides the option to duplicate a flow (added in [0.5.0](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#03%2F07%2F2025-0-5-0)<br>) |
| embedding.locale | ❌   | `en` \| `nl` \| `de` \| `fr` \| `es` \| `ja` \| `zh` \| `pt` \| `zh-TW` \| `ru` \| | it takes [ISO 639-1](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_ISO_639_language_codes)<br> locale codes (added in [0.5.0](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/sdk-changelog#03%2F07%2F2025-0-5-0)<br>) |
| navigation.handler | ❌   | `({route:string}) => void` | This callback will be triggered each time a route in Activepieces changes, you can read more about it [here](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/navigation) |

For the font to be loaded, you need to set both the `fontUrl` and `fontFamily` properties. If you only set one of them, the default font will be used. The default font is `Roboto`. The font weights we use are the default font-weights from [tailwind](https://tailwindcss.com/docs/font-weight)
.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/embedding/embed-builder.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/embedding/embed-builder)

[Provision Users](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/provision-users)
[Show/Hide Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/customize-pieces)

# Navigation - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/navigation#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Misc

Navigation

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Automatically Sync URL](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/navigation#automatically-sync-url)
    
*   [Navigate Method](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/navigation#navigate-method)
    
*   [Navigate to Initial Route](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/navigation#navigate-to-initial-route)
    

By default, navigating within your embedded instance of Activepieces doesn’t affect the client’s browser history or viewed URL. Activepieces only provide a **handler**, that trigger on every route change in the **iframe**.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/navigation#automatically-sync-url)

Automatically Sync URL
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can use the following snippet when configuring the SDK, which will implement a handler that syncs the Activepieces iframe with your browser:

The following snippet listens when the user clicks backward, so it syncs the route back to the iframe using `activepieces.navigate` and in the handler, it updates the URL of the browser.

    const instanceUrl = 'YOUR_INSTANCE_URL';
    const jwtToken = 'YOUR_GENERATED_JWT_TOKEN';
    const containerId = 'YOUR_CONTAINER_ID';
    activepieces.configure({
      instanceUrl,
      jwtToken,
      embedding: {
        containerId,
        builder: {
          disableNavigation: false,
          hideFlowName: false
        },
        dashboard: {
          hideSidebar: false
        },
        hideFolders: false,
        navigation: {
          handler: ({ route }) => {
            //route can include search params at the end of it
            if (!window.location.href.endsWith(route)) {
              window.history.pushState({}, "", window.location.origin + route);
            }
          }
        }
      },
    });
    
    window.addEventListener("popstate", () => {
      const route = activepieces.extractActivepiecesRouteFromUrl({ vendorUrl: window.location.href });
      activepieces.navigate({ route });
    });
    

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/navigation#navigate-method)

Navigate Method
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you use `activepieces.navigate({ route: '/flows' })` this will tell the embedded sdk where to navigate to. Here is the list for routes the sdk can navigate to:

| Route | Description |
| --- | --- |
| `/flows` | Flows table |
| `/flows/{flowId}` | Opens up a flow in the builder |
| `/runs` | Runs table |
| `/runs/{runId}` | Opens up a run in the builder |
| `/connections` | Connections table |
| `/tables` | Tables table |
| `/tables/{tableId}` | Opens up a table |
| `todos` | Todos table |
| `todos/{todoId}` | Opens up a todo |

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/navigation#navigate-to-initial-route)

Navigate to Initial Route
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can call the `navigate` method after initializing the sdk using the `configure` sdk:

    const flowId = '1234';
    const instanceUrl = 'YOUR_INSTANCE_URL';
    const jwtToken = 'YOUR_GENERATED_JWT_TOKEN';
    activepieces.configure({
    	instanceUrl,
    	jwtToken,
    }).then(() => {
    	activepieces.navigate({
    		route: `/flows/${flowId}`
    	})
    });
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/embedding/navigation.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/embedding/navigation)

[Create/Update Connections](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/embed-connections)
[Predefined Connection](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/predefined-connection)

⌘I

Project Members

Project Member Schema

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

Example

    {
      "id": "<string>",
      "created": "<string>",
      "updated": "<string>",
      "platformId": "<string>",
      "userId": "<string>",
      "projectId": "<string>",
      "projectRoleId": "<string>"
    }

Project member is which user is assigned to a project.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/project-members/schema#schema-id)

id

string

required

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/project-members/schema#schema-created)

created

string

required

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/project-members/schema#schema-updated)

updated

string

required

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/project-members/schema#schema-platform-id)

platformId

string

required

Pattern: `^[0-9a-zA-Z]{21}$`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/project-members/schema#schema-user-id)

userId

string

required

Pattern: `^[0-9a-zA-Z]{21}$`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/project-members/schema#schema-project-id)

projectId

string

required

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/project-members/schema#schema-project-role-id)

projectRoleId

string

required

Pattern: `^[0-9a-zA-Z]{21}$`

[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/endpoints/project-members/schema)

Git Sync

Configure

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

cURL

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://cloud.activepieces.com/api/v1/git-repos \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "projectId": "<string>",
      "remoteUrl": "<string>",
      "branch": "<string>",
      "branchType": "PRODUCTION",
      "sshPrivateKey": "<string>",
      "slug": "<string>"
    }
    '

201

    {
      "id": "<string>",
      "created": "<string>",
      "updated": "<string>",
      "remoteUrl": "<string>",
      "branch": "<string>",
      "branchType": "PRODUCTION",
      "projectId": "<string>",
      "slug": "<string>"
    }

/

v1

/

git-repos

Try it

cURL

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://cloud.activepieces.com/api/v1/git-repos \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "projectId": "<string>",
      "remoteUrl": "<string>",
      "branch": "<string>",
      "branchType": "PRODUCTION",
      "sshPrivateKey": "<string>",
      "slug": "<string>"
    }
    '

201

    {
      "id": "<string>",
      "created": "<string>",
      "updated": "<string>",
      "remoteUrl": "<string>",
      "branch": "<string>",
      "branchType": "PRODUCTION",
      "projectId": "<string>",
      "slug": "<string>"
    }

#### Body

application/json

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/git-repos/configure#body-project-id)

projectId

string

required

Minimum string length: `1`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/git-repos/configure#body-remote-url)

remoteUrl

string

required

Pattern: `^git@`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/git-repos/configure#body-branch)

branch

string

required

Minimum string length: `1`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/git-repos/configure#body-branch-type-one-of-0)

branchType

Option 1 · enum<string>Option 2 · enum<string>Option 1 · enum<string>Option 2 · enum<string>

required

Available options:

`PRODUCTION`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/git-repos/configure#body-ssh-private-key)

sshPrivateKey

string

required

Minimum string length: `1`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/git-repos/configure#body-slug)

slug

string

required

Minimum string length: `1`

#### Response

201 - application/json

Default Response

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/git-repos/configure#response-id)

id

string

required

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/git-repos/configure#response-created)

created

string

required

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/git-repos/configure#response-updated)

updated

string

required

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/git-repos/configure#response-remote-url)

remoteUrl

string

required

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/git-repos/configure#response-branch)

branch

string

required

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/git-repos/configure#response-branch-type-one-of-0)

branchType

Option 1 · enum<string>Option 2 · enum<string>Option 1 · enum<string>Option 2 · enum<string>

required

Available options:

`PRODUCTION`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/git-repos/configure#response-project-id)

projectId

string

required

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/git-repos/configure#response-slug)

slug

string

required

cURL

cURL

    curl --request POST \
      --url https://cloud.activepieces.com/api/v1/project-releases \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "type": "ROLLBACK",
      "name": "<string>",
      "projectId": "<string>",
      "projectReleaseId": "<string>",
      "description": "<string>",
      "selectedFlowsIds": [\
        "<string>"\
      ]
    }
    '

201

    {
      "id": "<string>",
      "created": "<string>",
      "updated": "<string>",
      "projectId": "<string>",
      "name": "<string>",
      "fileId": "<string>",
      "type": "GIT",
      "description": "<string>",
      "importedBy": "<string>",
      "importedByUser": {
        "id": "<string>",
        "email": "<string>",
        "firstName": "<string>",
        "status": "ACTIVE",
        "platformRole": "ADMIN",
        "lastName": "<string>",
        "created": "<string>",
        "updated": "<string>",
        "externalId": "<string>",
        "platformId": "<string>",
        "lastActiveDate": "<string>",
        "imageUrl": "<string>"
      }
    }

# Building Flows - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/building-flows#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

Navigation

Flows

Building Flows

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Trigger](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/building-flows#trigger)
    
*   [Action](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/building-flows#action)
    

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/building-flows#trigger)

Trigger
------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The flow’s starting point determines its frequency of execution. There are various types of triggers available, such as Schedule Trigger, Webhook Trigger, or Event Trigger based on specific service.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/building-flows#action)

Action
----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Actions come after the flow and control what occurs when the flow is activated, like running code or communicating with other services. In real-life scenario: ![Flow Parts](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP/resources/flow-parts.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP&q=85&s=8cfbbe303a83429b453e40a0fa4af0af)

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/flows/building-flows.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/flows/building-flows)

[Welcome](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Passing Data](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data)

cURL

      --url https://cloud.activepieces.com/api/v1/flows/{id} \

      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "type": "MOVE_ACTION",
      "request": {
        "name": "<string>",
        "newParentStep": "<string>",
        "stepLocationRelativeToNewParent": "AFTER",
        "branchIndex": 123
      }
    }
    '

string

required

#### Body

application/json

*   Move Action
    
*   Change Status
    
*   Lock and Publish
    
*   Copy as Draft
    
*   Lock Flow
    
*   Import Flow
    
*   Change Name
    
*   Delete Action
    
*   Update Action
    
*   Add Action
    
*   Update Trigger
    
*   Change Folder
    
*   Duplicate Action
    
*   Delete Branch
    
*   Add Branch
    
*   Duplicate Branch
    
*   Skip Action
    
*   Update Metadata
    
*   Option 19
    
*   Option 20
    
*   Update Minutes Saved
    
*   Update Owner
    
*   Update Note
    
*   Delete Note
    
*   Add Note

required

`MOVE_ACTION`

# Debugging Runs - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/debugging-runs#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Flows

Debugging Runs

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

You can monitor each run that results from an enabled flow:

1.  Go to the Dashboard, click on **Runs**.
2.  Find the run that you’re looking for, and click on it.
3.  You will see the builder in a view-only mode, each step will show a ✅ or a ❌ to indicate its execution status.
4.  Click on any of these steps, you will see the **input** and **output** in the **Run Details** panel.

The debugging experience looks like this: ![Debugging Business Automations](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/screenshots/using-activepieces-debugging.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-&q=85&s=10c28d9178fdca26e71567b0278dff3d)

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/flows/debugging-runs.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/flows/debugging-runs)

[Publishing Flows](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/publishing-flows)
[Version History](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/versioning)

      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \

          },\

        }\

    }

# Development setup - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Build a Piece

Development setup

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Prerequisites](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup#prerequisites)
    
*   [Instructions](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup#instructions)
    
*   [Pieces Development](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup#pieces-development)
    

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Node.js v18+
*   npm v9+

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup#instructions)

Instructions
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Setup the environment

    node tools/setup-dev.js
    

2.  Start the environment

This command will start activepieces with sqlite3 and in memory queue.

    npm start
    

By default, the development setup only builds specific pieces.Open the file `.env.dev` and add comma-separated list of pieces to make available.For more details, check out the [Piece Development](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup#pieces-development)
 section.

3.  Go to _**localhost:4200**_ on your web browser and sign in with these details:

Email: `[[email protected]](https://www.activepieces.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ` Password: `12345678`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup#pieces-development)

Pieces Development
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When [`AP_PIECES_SYNC_MODE`](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/blob/main/.env.dev#L14)
 is set to `OFFICIAL_AUTO`, all pieces are automatically loaded from the cloud API and synced to the database on first launch. This process may take a few seconds to several minutes depending on your internet connection. For local development, pieces are loaded from your local `dist` folder instead of the database. To enable this, set the [`AP_DEV_PIECES`](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/blob/main/.env.dev#L5)
 environment variable with a comma-separated list of pieces. For example, to develop with `google-sheets` and `cal-com`:

    AP_DEV_PIECES=google-sheets,cal-com npm start
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup)

[Fork Repository](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/setup-fork)
[Create Piece Definition](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/piece-definition)

⌘I

---

# Create Piece Definition - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/piece-definition#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Build a Piece

Create Piece Definition

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Piece Definition](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/piece-definition#piece-definition)
    

This tutorial will guide you through the process of creating a Gelato piece with an action that fetches random icecream flavor and trigger that fetches new icecream flavor created. It assumes that you are familiar with the following:

*   [Activepieces Local development](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup)
     Or [GitHub Codespaces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/misc/codespaces)
    .
*   TypeScript syntax.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/piece-definition#piece-definition)

Piece Definition
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To get started, let’s generate a new piece for Gelato

    npm run cli pieces create
    

You will be asked three questions to define your new piece:

1.  `Piece Name`: Specify a name for your piece. This name uniquely identifies your piece within the ActivePieces ecosystem.
2.  `Package Name`: Optionally, you can enter a name for the npm package associated with your piece. If left blank, the default name will be used.
3.  `Piece Type`: Choose the piece type based on your intention. It can be either “custom” if it’s a tailored solution for your needs, or “community” if it’s designed to be shared and used by the broader community.

**Example:**

    npm run cli pieces create
    
    ? Enter the piece name: gelato
    ? Enter the package name: @activepieces/piece-gelato
    ? Select the piece type: community
    

The piece will be generated at `packages/pieces/community/gelato/`, the `src/index.ts` file should contain the following code

    import { PieceAuth, createPiece } from '@activepieces/pieces-framework';
    
    export const gelato = createPiece({
      displayName: 'Gelato',
      logoUrl: 'https://cdn.activepieces.com/pieces/gelato.png',
      auth: PieceAuth.None(),
      authors: [],
      actions: [],
      triggers: [],
    });
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/piece-definition.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/build-pieces/building-pieces/piece-definition)

[Development setup](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup)
[Add Piece Authentication](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/piece-authentication)

⌘I

# Add Piece Authentication - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/piece-authentication#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Build a Piece

Add Piece Authentication

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Piece Authentication](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/piece-authentication#piece-authentication)
    

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/piece-authentication#piece-authentication)

Piece Authentication

Activepieces supports multiple forms of authentication, you can check those forms [here](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/authentication)
 Now, let’s establish authentication for this piece, which necessitates the inclusion of an API Key in the headers. Modify `src/index.ts` file to add authentication,

    import { PieceAuth, createPiece } from '@activepieces/pieces-framework';
    
    export const gelatoAuth = PieceAuth.SecretText({
      displayName: 'API Key',
      required: true,
      description: 'Please use **test-key** as value for API Key',
    });
    
    export const gelato = createPiece({
      displayName: 'Gelato',
      logoUrl: 'https://cdn.activepieces.com/pieces/gelato.png',
      auth: gelatoAuth,
      authors: [],
      actions: [],
      triggers: [],
    });
    

Use the value **test-key** as the API key when testing actions or triggers for Gelato.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/piece-authentication.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/build-pieces/building-pieces/piece-authentication)

[Create Piece Definition](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/piece-definition)
[Create Action](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/create-action)

⌘I

On this page

*   [Steps to setup Codespaces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/misc/codespaces#steps-to-setup-codespaces)
    

GitHub Codespaces is a cloud development platform that enables developers to write, run, and debug code directly in their browsers, seamlessly integrated with GitHub.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/misc/codespaces#steps-to-setup-codespaces)

Steps to setup Codespaces

1.  Go to [Activepieces repo](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces)
    .
2.  Click Code `<>`, then under codespaces click create codespace on main.

![Create Codespace](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP/resources/screenshots/development-setup_codespaces.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP&q=85&s=092a5f882369bd1b2ce25b92487d179d)

By default, the development setup only builds specific pieces.Open the file `.env.dev` and add comma-separated list of pieces to make available.For more details, check out the [Piece Development](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup#pieces-development)
 section.

3.  Open the terminal and run `npm start`
4.  Access the frontend URL by opening port 4200 and signing in with these details:

Email: `[[email protected]](https://www.activepieces.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ` Password: `12345678`

Build a Piece

Start Building

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Steps Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/start-building#steps-overview)
    

This section guides you in creating a Gelato piece, from setting up your development environment to contributing the piece. By the end of this tutorial, you will have a piece with an action that fetches a random ice cream flavor and a trigger that fetches newly created ice cream flavors.

These are the next sections. In each step, we will do one small thing. This tutorial should take around 30 minutes.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/start-building#steps-overview)

Steps Overview
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/start-building#)

Fork Repository

Fork the repository to create your own copy of the codebase.

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/start-building#)

Setup Development Environment

Set up your development environment with the necessary tools and dependencies.

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/start-building#)

Create Piece Definition

Define the structure and behavior of your Gelato piece.

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/start-building#)

Add Piece Authentication

Implement authentication mechanisms for your Gelato piece.

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/start-building#)

Create Action

Create an action that fetches a random ice cream flavor.

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/start-building#)

Create Trigger

Create a trigger that fetches newly created ice cream flavors.

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/start-building#)

Sharing Pieces

Share your Gelato piece with others.

Contribution
------------

Contribute a piece to our repo and receive +1,400 tasks/month on [Activepieces Cloud](https://cloud.activepieces.com/)
.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/start-building.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/build-pieces/building-pieces/start-building)

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)

# Version History - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/versioning#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Flows

Version History

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

Activepieces keeps track of all published flows and their versions. Here’s how it works:

1.  You can edit a flow as many times as you want in **draft** mode.
2.  Once you’re done with your changes, you can publish it.
3.  The published version will be locked and uneditable.
4.  If you try to edit a published flow, Activepieces will create a new **draft** if there is none and copy the **published** version to the new version.

This means you can always go back to a previous version and edit the flow in draft mode without affecting the published version. ![Flow History](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/31xTG5PE4V5GpSM9/resources/screenshots/flow-history.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=31xTG5PE4V5GpSM9&q=85&s=24de78e342ce7672bc6ccb29c352940c) As you can see in the following screenshot, the yellow dot refers to DRAFT and the green dot refers to PUBLISHED.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/flows/versioning.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/flows/versioning)

[Debugging Runs](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/debugging-runs)
[Technical Limits](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/known-limits)

      --url https://cloud.activepieces.com/api/v1/projects/{id} \
      --header 'Authorization: Bearer <token>' \
      --header 'Content-Type: application/json' \
      --data '
    {
      "releasesEnabled": true,
      "displayName": "<string>",
      "externalId": "<string>",
      "metadata": {},
      "plan": {
        "pieces": [\
          "<string>"\
        ],
        "piecesFilterType": "NONE"
      }
    }
    '

# Community (Public NPM) - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/sharing-pieces/community#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Sharing Pieces

Community (Public NPM)

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

You can publish your pieces to the npm registry and share them with the community. Users can install your piece from Settings -> My Pieces -> Install Piece -> type in the name of your piece package.

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/sharing-pieces/community#)

Login to npm

Make sure you are logged in to npm. If not, please run:

    npm login
    

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/sharing-pieces/community#)

Rename Piece

Rename the piece name in `package.json` to something unique or related to your organization’s scope (e.g., `@my-org/piece-PIECE_NAME`). You can find it at `packages/pieces/PIECE_NAME/package.json`.

Don’t forget to increase the version number in `package.json` for each new release.

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/sharing-pieces/community#)

Publish

Replace `PIECE_FOLDER_NAME` with the name of the folder.

Run the following command:

    npm run publish-piece PIECE_FOLDER_NAME
    

**Congratulations! You can now import the piece from the settings page.**

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/build-pieces/sharing-pieces/community.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/build-pieces/sharing-pieces/community)

[Contribute](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/sharing-pieces/contribute)
[Private](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/sharing-pieces/private)

⌘I

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/misc/dev-container#using-dev-containers-in-visual-studio-code)

Using Dev Containers in Visual Studio Code
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The project includes a dev container configuration that allows you to use Visual Studio Code’s [Remote Development](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=ms-vscode-remote.vscode-remote-extensionpack)
 extension to develop the project in a consistent environment. This can be especially helpful if you are new to the project or if you have a different environment setup on your local machine.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/misc/dev-container#prerequisites)

Prerequisites
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before you can use the dev container, you will need to install the following:

*   [Visual Studio Code](https://code.visualstudio.com/)
    .
*   The [Remote Development](https://marketplace.visualstudio.com/items?itemName=ms-vscode-remote.vscode-remote-extensionpack)
     extension for Visual Studio Code.
*   [Docker](https://www.docker.com/)
    .

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/misc/dev-container#using-the-dev-container)

Using the Dev Container
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To use the dev container for the Activepieces project, follow these steps:

1.  Clone the Activepieces repository to your local machine.
2.  Open the project in Visual Studio Code.
3.  Press `Ctrl+Shift+P` and type `> Dev Containers: Reopen in Container`.
4.  Run `npm start`.
5.  The backend will run at `localhost:3000` and the frontend will run at `localhost:4200`.

By default, the development setup only builds specific pieces.Open the file `.env.dev` and add comma-separated list of pieces to make available.For more details, check out the [Piece Development](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup#pieces-development)
 section.

The login credentials are:  
Email: `[[email protected]](https://www.activepieces.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) ` Password: `12345678`

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/misc/dev-container#exiting-the-dev-container)

Exiting the Dev Container
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To exit the dev container and return to your local environment, follow these steps:

1.  In the bottom left corner of Visual Studio Code, click the `Remote-Containers: Reopen folder locally` button.
2.  Visual Studio Code will close the connection to the dev container and reopen the project in your local environment.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/misc/dev-container#troubleshoot)

Troubleshoot
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

One of the best trouble shoot after an error occur is to reset the dev container.

1.  Exit the dev container
2.  Run the following
    
        sh tools/reset-dev.sh
        
    
3.  Rebuild the dev container from above steps

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/build-pieces/misc/dev-container.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/build-pieces/misc/dev-container)

[Testing Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/misc/testing-pieces)
[GitHub Codespaces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/misc/codespaces)

⌘I

# Passing Data - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Flows

Passing Data

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Data flow](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#data-flow)
    
*   [Example Steps](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#example-steps)
    
*   [Data to Insert Panel](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#data-to-insert-panel)
    
*   [Testing Steps to Generate Data](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#testing-steps-to-generate-data)
    
*   [Advanced Tips](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#advanced-tips)
    
*   [Switching to Dynamic Values](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#switching-to-dynamic-values)
    
*   [Accessing data by path](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#accessing-data-by-path)
    

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#data-flow)

Data flow
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Any Activepieces flow is a vertical diagram that **starts with a trigger step** followed by **any number of action steps**. Steps are connected vertically. Data flows from parent steps to the children. Children steps have access to the output data of the parent steps.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#example-steps)

Example Steps
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This flow has 3 steps, they can access data as follows:

*   **Step 1** is the main data producer to be used in the next steps. Data produced by Step 1 will be accessible in Steps 2 and 3. Some triggers don’t produce data though, like Schedules.
*   **Step 2** can access data produced by Step 1. After execution, this step will also produce data to be used in the next step(s).
*   **Step 3** can access data produced by Steps 1 and 2 as they’re its parent steps. This step can produce data but since it’s the last step in the flow, it can’t be used by other ones.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#data-to-insert-panel)

Data to Insert Panel
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In order to use data from a previous step in your current step, place your cursor in any input, the **Data to Insert** panel will pop up. This panel shows the accessible steps and their data. You can expand the data items to view their content, and you can click the items to insert them in your current settings input. If an item in this panel has a caret (⌄) to the right, it means you can click on the item to expand its child properties. You can select the parent item or its properties as you need. When you insert data from this panel, it gets inserted at the cursor’s position in the input. This means you can combine static text and dynamic data in any field. We generally recommend that you expand the items before inserting them to understand the type of data they contain and whether they’re the right fit to the input you’re filling.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#testing-steps-to-generate-data)

Testing Steps to Generate Data
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We require you to test steps before accessing their data. This approach protects you from selecting the wrong data and breaking your flows after publishing them. If a step is not tested and you try to access its data, you will see the following message: ![Test your automation step first](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP/resources/passing-data-test-step-first.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP&q=85&s=d5fdea437c038655acd7b9976c6309bc) To fix this, go to the step and use the Generate Sample Data panel to test it. Steps use different approaches for testing. These are the common ones:

*   **Load Data:** Some triggers will let you load data from your connected account without having to perform any action in that account.
*   **Test Trigger:** Some triggers will require you to head to your connected account and fire the trigger in order to generate sample data.
*   **Send Data:** Webhooks require you to send a sample request to the webhook URL to generate sample data.
*   **Test Action:** Action steps will let you run the action in order to generate sample data.

Follow the instructions in the Generate Sample Data panel to know how your step should be tested. Some triggers will also let you Use Mock Data, which will generate static sample data from the piece. We recommend that you test the step instead of using mock data. This is an example for generating sample data for a trigger using the **Load Data** button:

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#advanced-tips)

Advanced Tips
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#switching-to-dynamic-values)

Switching to Dynamic Values

Dropdowns and some other input types don’t let you select data from previous steps. If you’d like to bypass this and use data from previous steps instead, switch the input into a dynamic one using this button:

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/passing-data#accessing-data-by-path)

Accessing data by path

If you can’t find the data you’re looking for in the **Data to Insert** panel but you’d like to use it, you can write a JSON path instead. Use the following syntax to write JSON paths: `{{step_slug.path.to.property}}` The `step_slug` can be found by moving your cursor over any of your flow steps, it will show to the right of the step.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/flows/passing-data.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/flows/passing-data)

[Building Flows](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/building-flows)
[Publishing Flows](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/flows/publishing-flows)

⌘I

# External Libraries - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/external-libraries#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Piece Reference

External Libraries

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Dependency Pinning](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/external-libraries#dependency-pinning)
    

The Activepieces repository is structured as a monorepo, employing Nx as its build tool. To keep our main `package.json` as light as possible, we keep libraries that are only used for a piece in the piece `package.json` . This means when adding a new library you should navigate to the piece folder and install the library with our package manager `bun`

    cd packages/pieces/<piece-path> 
    bun install --save <library-name>
    

*   Import the library into your piece.

Guidelines:

*   Make sure you are using well-maintained libraries.
*   Ensure that the library size is not too large to avoid bloating the bundle size; this will make the piece load faster in the sandbox.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/external-libraries#dependency-pinning)

Dependency Pinning
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When pieces are built for publishing, all dependency versions — including **transitive dependencies** (dependencies of your dependencies) — are automatically pinned to the exact versions resolved in the monorepo’s `bun.lock` file. This means:

*   You don’t need to worry about manually pinning transitive dependency versions.
*   The published piece will always install the same dependency tree that was tested during development.
*   This protects against supply chain attacks where a compromised transitive dependency could be silently pulled in at install time.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/external-libraries.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/build-pieces/piece-reference/external-libraries)

[Files](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/files)
[Piece Versioning](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/piece-versioning)

# Fork Repository - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/setup-fork#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Build a Piece

Fork Repository

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

To start building pieces, we need to fork the repository that contains the framework library and the development environment. Later, we will publish these pieces as `npm` artifacts. Follow these steps to fork the repository:

If you are on windows, please install [WSL](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/wsl/install)
 and set up git there then proceed with the instructions down below

1.  Go to the repository page at [https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces)
    .
2.  Click the `Fork` button located in the top right corner of the page.

![Fork Repository](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-/resources/screenshots/fork-repository.jpg?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=uHZ35vXyxX7goNO-&q=85&s=fa912e2c0634a5662761334495521976)

3.  Clone your fork using a shallow clone for faster setup:

    git clone --depth=1 https://github.com/YOUR_USERNAME/activepieces.git
    

Using `--depth=1` reduces the clone size significantly by only fetching the latest commit instead of the full history.

If you are an enterprise customer and want to use the private pieces feature, you can refer to the tutorial on how to set up a [private fork](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/misc/private-fork)
.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/setup-fork.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/build-pieces/building-pieces/setup-fork)

[Start Building](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/start-building)
[Development setup](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/development-setup)
