# How to Setup S3 - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/guides/setup-s3#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Guides

How to Setup S3

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Environment Variables](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/guides/setup-s3#environment-variables)
    

Run logs and files are stored in the database by default, but you can switch to S3 later without any migration; for most cases, the database is enough. It’s recommended to start with the database and switch to S3 if needed. After switching, expired files in the database will be deleted, and everything will be stored in S3. No manual migration is needed.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/guides/setup-s3#environment-variables)

Environment Variables
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Variable | Description | Default Value | Example |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `AP_FILE_STORAGE_LOCATION` | The location to store files. Set to `S3` for S3 storage. | `DB` | `S3` |
| `AP_S3_ACCESS_KEY_ID` | The access key ID for your S3-compatible storage service. Not required if `AP_S3_USE_IRSA` is `true`. | None |     |
| `AP_S3_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY` | The secret access key for your S3-compatible storage service. Not required if `AP_S3_USE_IRSA` is `true`. | None |     |
| `AP_S3_BUCKET` | The name of the S3 bucket to use for file storage. | None |     |
| `AP_S3_ENDPOINT` | The endpoint URL for your S3-compatible storage service. Not required if `AWS_ENDPOINT_URL` is set. | None | `https://s3.amazonaws.com` |
| `AP_S3_REGION` | The region where your S3 bucket is located. Not required if `AWS_REGION` is set. | None | `us-east-1` |
| `AP_S3_USE_SIGNED_URLS` | Routes file traffic directly to S3 using pre-signed URLs, bypassing the API server. The bucket should remain private; signed URLs provide temporary authenticated access. | None | `true` |
| `AP_S3_USE_IRSA` | Use IAM Role for Service Accounts (IRSA) to connect to S3. When `true`, `AP_S3_ACCESS_KEY_ID` and `AP_S3_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY` are not required. | None | `true` |
| `AP_MAX_FILE_SIZE_MB` | The maximum allowed file size in megabytes for uploads including logs of flow runs. | `10` | `10` |

**Friendly Tip #1**: If the S3 bucket supports signed URLs but needs to be accessible over a public network, you can set `AP_S3_USE_SIGNED_URLS` to `true` to route traffic directly to S3 and reduce heavy traffic on your API server.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/install/guides/setup-s3.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/install/guides/setup-s3)

[How to Setup OpenTelemetry](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/guides/setup-opentelemetry)
[How to Separate Workers](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/guides/separate-workers)

# Websocket Issues - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/websocket-issues#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Troubleshooting

Websocket Issues

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

If you’re experiencing issues with websocket connections, it’s likely due to incorrect proxy configuration. Common symptoms include:

*   Test Flow button not working
*   Test step in flows not working
*   Real-time updates not showing

To resolve these issues:

1.  Ensure your reverse proxy is properly configured for websocket connections
2.  Check our [Setup HTTPS](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/guides/setup-ssl)
     guide for correct configuration examples
3.  Some browsers block http websocket connections, please setup SSL to resolve this issue.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/install/troubleshooting/websocket-issues.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/install/troubleshooting/websocket-issues)

[Truncated Logs](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/truncated-logs)
[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/overview)

# Reset Password - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/reset-password#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Troubleshooting

Reset Password

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

If you forgot your password on a self-hosted instance, you can reset it using the following steps:

1.  **Locate PostgreSQL Docker Container**:
    *   Use a command like `docker ps` to find the PostgreSQL container.
2.  **Access the Container**:
    
    *   Use SSH to access the PostgreSQL Docker container.
    
        docker exec -it POSTGRES_CONTAINER_ID /bin/bash
        
    
3.  **Open the PostgreSQL Console**:
    
    *   Inside the container, open the PostgreSQL console with the `psql` command.
    
        psql -U postgres
        
    
4.  **Connect to the ActivePieces Database**:
    
    *   Connect to the ActivePieces database.
    
        \c activepieces
        
    
5.  **Create a Secure Password**:
    *   Use a tool like [bcrypt-generator.com](https://bcrypt-generator.com/)
         to generate a new secure password, number of rounds is 10.
6.  **Update Your Password**:
    
    *   Run the following SQL query within the PostgreSQL console, replacing `HASH_PASSWORD` with your new password and `YOUR_EMAIL_ADDRESS` with your email.
    
        UPDATE public.user_identity SET password='HASH_PASSWORD' WHERE email='YOUR_EMAIL_ADDRESS';
        
    

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/install/troubleshooting/reset-password.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/install/troubleshooting/reset-password)

[Queues Dashboard](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard)
[Truncated Logs](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/truncated-logs)

⌘I

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#discovery)

Discovery
-----------------------------------------------------------------------

These tools are always available (locked) and read-only. They help AI agents understand what’s in the project before making changes.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_list_flows)

ap\_list\_flows

List all flows in the current project.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| —   | —   | —   | No inputs required |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_flow_structure)

ap\_flow\_structure

Get the structure of a flow: step tree, configuration status, and valid insert locations.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowId` | string | Yes | The flow ID |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_list_pieces)

ap\_list\_pieces

List available pieces with their actions and triggers. Required before adding or updating steps.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `searchQuery` | string | No  | Filter pieces by name |
| `includeActions` | boolean | No  | Include action details |
| `includeTriggers` | boolean | No  | Include trigger details |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_list_connections)

ap\_list\_connections

List OAuth/app connections in the project. Required before adding steps that need authentication.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| —   | —   | —   | No inputs required |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_list_ai_models)

ap\_list\_ai\_models

List configured AI providers and their available models. Use this to discover valid `aiProviderModel` values for configuring Run Agent steps.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `provider` | string | No  | Filter by provider (`openai`, `anthropic`, `google`, `azure`, `openrouter`, `activepieces`, `cloudflare-gateway`, `custom`) |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_list_tables)

ap\_list\_tables

List all tables in the project with their fields (name, type, id) and row counts.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| —   | —   | —   | No inputs required |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_find_records)

ap\_find\_records

Query records from a table with optional filtering.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `tableId` | string | Yes | The table ID |
| `filters` | array | No  | Filter conditions (fieldName, operator, value) |
| `limit` | number | No  | Max records (default 50, max 500) |

**Filter operators:** `eq`, `neq`, `gt`, `gte`, `lt`, `lte`, `co` (contains), `exists`, `not_exists`

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_list_runs)

ap\_list\_runs

List recent flow runs with optional filters.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowId` | string | No  | Filter by flow |
| `status` | string | No  | Filter by status (SUCCEEDED, FAILED, RUNNING, etc.) |
| `limit` | number | No  | Max runs (default 10, max 50) |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_get_run)

ap\_get\_run

Get detailed results of a flow run including step-by-step outputs, errors, and durations.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowRunId` | string | Yes | The run ID |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_setup_guide)

ap\_setup\_guide

Get step-by-step instructions for setting up connections or AI providers. Returns instructions for the user to follow in the UI — credentials are never handled through MCP.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `topic` | string | Yes | `connection` or `ai_provider` |
| `pieceName` | string | No  | For connections: which piece needs auth |

* * *

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#flow-management)

Flow Management
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Create and manage flows.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_create_flow)

ap\_create\_flow

Create a new empty flow.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowName` | string | Yes | Display name for the flow |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_rename_flow)

ap\_rename\_flow

Rename an existing flow.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowId` | string | Yes | The flow ID |
| `displayName` | string | Yes | New name |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_change_flow_status)

ap\_change\_flow\_status

Enable or disable a flow.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowId` | string | Yes | The flow ID |
| `status` | string | Yes | `ENABLED` or `DISABLED` |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_lock_and_publish)

ap\_lock\_and\_publish

Publish the current draft of a flow. Validates all steps are configured.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowId` | string | Yes | The flow ID |

* * *

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#flow-building)

Flow Building
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Add, configure, and remove steps in a flow.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_update_trigger)

ap\_update\_trigger

Set or update the trigger for a flow.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowId` | string | Yes | The flow ID |
| `pieceName` | string | Yes | Piece name (e.g., `@activepieces/piece-gmail`) |
| `pieceVersion` | string | Yes | Piece version (e.g., `~0.11.6`) |
| `triggerName` | string | Yes | Trigger name from the piece |
| `input` | object | No  | Trigger configuration |
| `auth` | string | No  | Connection externalId |
| `displayName` | string | No  | Display name for the trigger step |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_add_step)

ap\_add\_step

Add a new step to a flow. Creates a skeleton — configure it with `ap_update_step`.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowId` | string | Yes | The flow ID |
| `parentStepName` | string | Yes | Step to insert after/into |
| `stepLocationRelativeToParent` | string | Yes | `AFTER`, `INSIDE_LOOP`, or `INSIDE_BRANCH` |
| `stepType` | string | Yes | `CODE`, `PIECE`, `LOOP_ON_ITEMS`, or `ROUTER` |
| `displayName` | string | Yes | Step display name |
| `pieceName` | string | No  | For PIECE steps |
| `pieceVersion` | string | No  | For PIECE steps |
| `actionName` | string | No  | For PIECE steps |
| `branchIndex` | number | No  | For INSIDE\_BRANCH |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_update_step)

ap\_update\_step

Update an existing step’s settings. Auto-fills default values for optional properties.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowId` | string | Yes | The flow ID |
| `stepName` | string | Yes | Step name (e.g., `step_1`) |
| `displayName` | string | No  | New display name |
| `input` | object | No  | Step configuration |
| `auth` | string | No  | Connection externalId |
| `actionName` | string | No  | For PIECE steps |
| `loopItems` | string | No  | For LOOP steps |
| `skip` | boolean | No  | Skip this step |

Use `{{stepName.output.field}}` syntax in input values to reference data from previous steps.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_delete_step)

ap\_delete\_step

Delete a step from a flow.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowId` | string | Yes | The flow ID |
| `stepName` | string | Yes | Step to delete |

* * *

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#router-&-branching)

Router & Branching
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Manage conditional branches in router steps.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_add_branch)

ap\_add\_branch

Add a conditional branch to a router step.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowId` | string | Yes | The flow ID |
| `stepName` | string | Yes | The router step name |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_delete_branch)

ap\_delete\_branch

Delete a branch from a router step.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowId` | string | Yes | The flow ID |
| `stepName` | string | Yes | The router step name |
| `branchIndex` | number | Yes | Which branch to delete |

* * *

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#annotations)

Annotations
---------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_manage_notes)

ap\_manage\_notes

Add, update, or delete canvas notes on a flow.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowId` | string | Yes | The flow ID |
| `operation` | string | Yes | `ADD`, `UPDATE`, or `DELETE` |
| `noteId` | string | No  | Required for UPDATE/DELETE |
| `content` | string | No  | Note text (required for ADD) |
| `color` | string | No  | Note color |
| `position` | object | No  | `{x, y}` canvas position |
| `size` | object | No  | `{width, height}` note dimensions (default 200x200) |

* * *

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#tables)

Tables
-----------------------------------------------------------------

Full CRUD operations for the built-in Tables feature. Use field names (not IDs) when inserting or updating records.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_create_table)

ap\_create\_table

Create a new table with an initial set of fields.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `name` | string | Yes | Table name |
| `fields` | array | Yes | Fields: `{name, type, options?}` |

**Field types:** `TEXT`, `NUMBER`, `DATE`, `STATIC_DROPDOWN` (requires `options` array)

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_delete_table)

ap\_delete\_table

Permanently delete a table and all its data.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `tableId` | string | Yes | The table ID |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_manage_fields)

ap\_manage\_fields

Add, rename, or delete fields on a table.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `tableId` | string | Yes | The table ID |
| `operation` | string | Yes | `ADD`, `UPDATE`, or `DELETE` |
| `fieldId` | string | No  | Required for UPDATE/DELETE |
| `name` | string | No  | Required for ADD/UPDATE |
| `type` | string | No  | Required for ADD |
| `options` | array | No  | For STATIC\_DROPDOWN |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_insert_records)

ap\_insert\_records

Insert one or more records into a table.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `tableId` | string | Yes | The table ID |
| `records` | array | Yes | 1-50 records, each mapping field names to values |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_update_record)

ap\_update\_record

Update specific cells in a record. Only specified fields are changed.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `tableId` | string | Yes | The table ID |
| `recordId` | string | Yes | The record ID |
| `fields` | object | Yes | Field names to new values |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_delete_records)

ap\_delete\_records

Permanently delete one or more records.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `recordIds` | array | Yes | Record IDs to delete |

* * *

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#testing-&-runs)

Testing & Runs
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Test flows, inspect results, and retry failures. Test tools poll for up to 120 seconds and return step-by-step results.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_test_flow)

ap\_test\_flow

Test a flow end-to-end in the test environment using saved sample data.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowId` | string | Yes | The flow ID |

The flow must have a configured trigger. The tool validates this before running and returns a clear error if not.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_test_step)

ap\_test\_step

Test a single step within a flow. Runs all steps up to and including the target step.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowId` | string | Yes | The flow ID |
| `stepName` | string | Yes | Step to test |

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/mcp/tools#ap_retry_run)

ap\_retry\_run

Retry a failed flow run.

| Input | Type | Required | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `flowRunId` | string | Yes | The failed run ID |
| `strategy` | string | Yes | `FROM_FAILED_STEP` or `ON_LATEST_VERSION` |

*   **FROM\_FAILED\_STEP**: Resume from where it failed, keeping previous step outputs
*   **ON\_LATEST\_VERSION**: Re-run the entire flow with the current published version

[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/mcp/tools)

[i18n Translations](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/about/i18n)

# Piece Auth - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/authentication#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Piece Reference

Piece Auth

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Secret Text](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/authentication#secret-text)
    
*   [Username and Password](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/authentication#username-and-password)
    
*   [Custom](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/authentication#custom)
    
*   [OAuth2](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/authentication#oauth2)
    

Piece authentication is used to gather user credentials and securely store them for future use in different flows. The authentication must be defined as the `auth` parameter in the `createPiece`, `createTrigger`, and `createAction` functions. This requirement ensures that the type of authentication can be inferred correctly in triggers and actions.

The auth parameter for `createPiece`, `createTrigger`, and `createAction` functions can take an array, but you cannot have more than one auth property of the same type, i.e two OAUTH2 properties.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/authentication#secret-text)

Secret Text

This authentication collects sensitive information, such as passwords or API keys. It is displayed as a masked input field. **Example:**

    PieceAuth.SecretText({
        displayName: 'API Key',
        description: 'Enter your API key',
        required: true,
        // Optional Validation
        validate: async ({auth}) => {
            if(auth.startsWith('sk_')){
                return {
                    valid: true,
                }
            }
            return {
                valid: false,
                error: 'Invalid Api Key'
            }
        }
    })
    

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/authentication#username-and-password)

Username and Password

This authentication collects a username and password as separate fields. **Example:**

    PieceAuth.BasicAuth({
        displayName: 'Credentials',
        description: 'Enter your username and password',
        required: true,
        username: {
            displayName: 'Username',
            description: 'Enter your username',
        },
        password: {
            displayName: 'Password',
            description: 'Enter your password',
        },
        // Optional Validation
        validate: async ({auth}) => {
            if(auth){
                return {
                    valid: true,
                }
            }
            return {
                valid: false,
                error: 'Invalid Api Key'
            }
        }
    })
    

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/authentication#custom)

Custom

This authentication allows for custom authentication by collecting specific properties, such as a base URL and access token. **Example:**

    PieceAuth.CustomAuth({
        displayName: 'Custom Authentication',
        description: 'Enter custom authentication details',
        props: {
            base_url: Property.ShortText({
                displayName: 'Base URL',
                description: 'Enter the base URL',
                required: true,
            }),
            access_token: PieceAuth.SecretText({
                displayName: 'Access Token',
                description: 'Enter the access token',
                required: true
            })
        },
        // Optional Validation
        validate: async ({auth}) => {
            if(auth){
                return {
                    valid: true,
                }
            }
            return {
                valid: false,
                error: 'Invalid Api Key'
            }
        },
        required: true
    })
    

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/authentication#oauth2)

OAuth2

This authentication collects OAuth2 authentication details, including the authentication URL, token URL, and scope. **Example:**

    PieceAuth.OAuth2({
        displayName: 'OAuth2 Authentication',
        grantType: OAuth2GrantType.AUTHORIZATION_CODE,
        required: true,
        authUrl: 'https://example.com/auth',
        tokenUrl: 'https://example.com/token',
        scope: ['read', 'write']
    })
    

Please note `OAuth2GrantType.CLIENT_CREDENTIALS` is also supported for service-based authentication.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/authentication.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/build-pieces/piece-reference/authentication)

[Private](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/sharing-pieces/private)
[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/piece-reference/triggers/overview)

⌘I

On this page

Engineers are the majority of the Activepieces team, and we are always looking for highly talented product engineers.

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/hiring/hiring#)

Technical Interview

Here, you’ll face a real challenge from Activepieces. We’ll guide you through it to see how you solve problems.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/hiring/hiring#)

Product & Leadership Interview

We’ll chat about your past experiences and how you design products. It’s like having a friendly conversation where we reflect on what you’ve done before.

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/hiring/hiring#)

Work Trial

You’ll do open source task for one day. This open source contribution task help us understand how well we work together.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/hiring/hiring#interviewing-tips)

Interviewing Tips
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every interview should make us say **HELL YES**. If not, we’ll kindly pass. **Avoid Bias:** Get opinions from others to make fair decisions. **Speak Up Early:** If you’re unsure about something, ask or test it right away.

# Engineering Workflow - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/onboarding/how-we-work#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Engineering Onboarding

Engineering Workflow

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Sprints](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/onboarding/how-we-work#sprints)
    
*   [Pull Requests](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/onboarding/how-we-work#pull-requests)
    
*   [Planning is everyone’s job.](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/onboarding/how-we-work#planning-is-everyone%E2%80%99s-job)
    

Activepieces work is based on one-week sprints, as priorities change fast, the sprint has to be short to adapt.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/onboarding/how-we-work#sprints)

Sprints
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sprints are shared publicly on our GitHub account. This would give everyone visibility into what we are working on.

*   There should be a GitHub issue for the sprint set up in advance that outlines the changes.
*   Each _individual_ should come prepared with specific suggestions for what they will work on over the next sprint. **if you’re in an engineering role, no one will dictate to you what to build – it is up to you to drive this.**
*   Teams generally meet once a week to pick the **priorities** together.
*   Everyone in the team should attend the sprint planning.
*   Anyone can comment on the sprint issue before or after the sprint.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/onboarding/how-we-work#pull-requests)

Pull Requests
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When it comes to code review, we have a few guidelines to ensure efficiency:

*   Create a pull request in draft state as soon as possible.
*   Be proactive and review other people’s pull requests. Don’t wait for someone to ask for your review; it’s your responsibility.
*   Assign only one reviewer to your pull request.
*   Add the PR to the current project (sprint) so we can keep track of unmerged PRs at the end of each sprint.
*   It is the **responsibility** of the **PR owner** to draft the test scenarios within the PR description. Upon review, the reviewer may assume that these scenarios have been tested and provide additional suggestions for scenarios.
*   Large, incomplete features should be broken down into smaller tasks and continuously merged into the main branch.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/onboarding/how-we-work#planning-is-everyone%E2%80%99s-job)

Planning is everyone’s job.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Every engineer is responsible for discovering bugs/opportunities and bringing them up in the sprint to convert them into actionable tasks.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/handbook/engineering/onboarding/how-we-work.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/handbook/engineering/onboarding/how-we-work)

[Onboarding Check List](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/onboarding/onboarding-check-list)
[On-Call](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/onboarding/on-call)

⌘I

# Database Migrations - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/database-migration#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Engineering Playbooks

Database Migrations

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Database Support](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/database-migration#database-support)
    
*   [Editions](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/database-migration#editions)
    
*   [How To Generate](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/database-migration#how-to-generate)
    
*   [PGlite Compatibility](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/database-migration#pglite-compatibility)
    

Activepieces uses TypeORM as its database driver in Node.js. We support two database types across different editions of our platform. The database migration files contain both what to do to migrate (up method) and what to do when rolling back (down method).

Read more about TypeORM migrations here: [https://orkhan.gitbook.io/typeorm/docs/migrations](https://orkhan.gitbook.io/typeorm/docs/migrations)

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/database-migration#database-support)

Database Support
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   PostgreSQL
*   PGlite

**Why Do we have PGlite?** We support PGlite to simplify development and self-hosting. It’s particularly helpful for:

*   Developers creating pieces who want a quick setup
*   Self-hosters using platforms to manage docker images but doesn’t support docker compose.

PGlite is a lightweight PostgreSQL implementation that runs embedded, so migrations are compatible with PostgreSQL.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/database-migration#editions)

Editions
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Enterprise & Cloud Edition** (Must use PostgreSQL)
*   **Community Edition** (Can use PostgreSQL or PGlite)

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/database-migration#how-to-generate)

How To Generate

1

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/database-migration#)

Setup AP\_DB\_TYPE

Set the `AP_DB_TYPE` environment variable to `POSTGRES` after making sure have latest state by running Activepieces first.

2

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/database-migration#)

Generate Migration

Run the migration generation command:

    npx turbo run db-migration --filter=api -- --name=<MIGRATION_NAME>
    

Replace `<MIGRATION_NAME>` with a descriptive name for your migration.

3

[](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/database-migration#)

Update Migration File

The command will generate a new migration file in `packages/server/api/src/app/database/migration/postgres/`.The generated file uses `MigrationInterface` — you need to update it:

1.  Change `implements MigrationInterface` to `implements Migration`
2.  Update the import from `typeorm` to import `Migration` from `../../migration`
3.  Add `breaking = false` (or `true` if the migration drops columns/tables or transforms data irreversibly)
4.  Add `release = '<version>'` matching the upcoming release version (check `package.json` in the repo root)
5.  Implement the `down()` method with queries that reverse the `up()` changes (unless `breaking = true`)
6.  Register it in `postgres-connection.ts`

    import { QueryRunner } from 'typeorm'
    import { Migration } from '../../migration'
    
    export class AddMyColumn1234567890 implements Migration {
        name = 'AddMyColumn1234567890'
        breaking = false
        release = '0.78.0'
    
        public async up(queryRunner: QueryRunner): Promise<void> {
            await queryRunner.query(`ALTER TABLE "project" ADD COLUMN "description" text`)
        }
    
        public async down(queryRunner: QueryRunner): Promise<void> {
            await queryRunner.query(`ALTER TABLE "project" DROP COLUMN "description"`)
        }
    }
    

CI will fail if `breaking`, `release`, or `down()` are missing on new migrations.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/database-migration#pglite-compatibility)

PGlite Compatibility
-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

While PGlite is mostly PostgreSQL-compatible, some features are not supported. When using features like `CONCURRENTLY` for index operations, you need to conditionally handle PGlite:

    import { QueryRunner } from 'typeorm'
    import { Migration } from '../../migration'
    import { system } from '../../../helper/system/system'
    import { AppSystemProp } from '../../../helper/system/system-props'
    import { DatabaseType } from '../../database-type'
    
    const databaseType = system.get(AppSystemProp.DB_TYPE)
    const isPGlite = databaseType === DatabaseType.PGLITE
    
    export class AddMyIndex1234567890 implements Migration {
        name = 'AddMyIndex1234567890'
        breaking = false
        release = '0.78.0'
        transaction = false // Required when using CONCURRENTLY
    
        public async up(queryRunner: QueryRunner): Promise<void> {
            if (isPGlite) {
                await queryRunner.query(`CREATE INDEX "idx_name" ON "table" ("column")`)
            } else {
                await queryRunner.query(`CREATE INDEX CONCURRENTLY "idx_name" ON "table" ("column")`)
            }
        }
    
        public async down(queryRunner: QueryRunner): Promise<void> {
            if (isPGlite) {
                await queryRunner.query(`DROP INDEX "idx_name"`)
            } else {
                await queryRunner.query(`DROP INDEX CONCURRENTLY "idx_name"`)
            }
        }
    }
    

`CREATE INDEX CONCURRENTLY` and `DROP INDEX CONCURRENTLY` are not supported in PGlite because PGLite is a single user/connection database. Always add a check for PGlite when using these operations.

Always test your migrations by running them both up and down to ensure they work as expected.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/database-migration.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/handbook/engineering/playbooks/database-migration)

[Cloud Infrastructure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/infrastructure)
[Feature Announcement](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/product-announcement)

⌘I

# Benchmark - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/benchmark#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Architecture

Benchmark

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [What’s Measured](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/benchmark#what%E2%80%99s-measured)
    
*   [Results](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/benchmark#results)
    
*   [Test Environment](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/benchmark#test-environment)
    
*   [How to Reproduce](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/benchmark#how-to-reproduce)
    
*   [Via GitHub Actions UI](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/benchmark#via-github-actions-ui)
    
*   [Via CLI](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/benchmark#via-cli)
    

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/benchmark#what%E2%80%99s-measured)

What’s Measured
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The benchmark tests end-to-end webhook flow execution: an HTTP request hits a **Catch Webhook** trigger, runs a **Code** action, and returns a response via **Return Response**. This measures the full request lifecycle including routing, execution, and response delivery.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/benchmark#results)

Results
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Configuration | Throughput (req/s) | Mean Latency | P50 | P99 |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| 1 App, 2 Workers | 95.1 | 20.8 ms | 15.4 ms | 62.7 ms |
| 2 Apps, 4 Workers | 167.6 | 23.4 ms | 20.0 ms | 65.1 ms |
| 3 Apps, 6 Workers | 231.8 | 24.8 ms | 21.2 ms | 71.5 ms |
| 1 App, 4 Workers | 174.5 | 22.4 ms | 19.0 ms | 56.7 ms |
| 2 Apps, 8 Workers | 286.5 | 26.0 ms | 22.3 ms | 89.5 ms |
| 3 Apps, 12 Workers | 336.6 | 35.1 ms | 34.8 ms | 51.5 ms |

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/benchmark#test-environment)

Test Environment
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Runner**: `depot-ubuntu-24.04-16` (16 cores)
*   **App container**: 2 CPU / 4 GB memory
*   **Worker container**: 0.5 CPU / 1 GB memory
*   **Execution mode**: `SANDBOX_CODE_ONLY`
*   **Rate limiter**: Disabled (`AP_PROJECT_RATE_LIMITER_ENABLED=false`)
*   **Total requests**: 500 per configuration

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/benchmark#how-to-reproduce)

How to Reproduce
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/benchmark#via-github-actions-ui)

Via GitHub Actions UI

1.  Go to the **Actions** tab in the repository
2.  Select the **Benchmark** workflow
3.  Click **Run workflow**
4.  Optionally adjust `total_requests` (default: 500)
5.  All 6 configurations (1:2 and 1:4 ratios at 1x/2x/3x scale) run in parallel automatically

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/benchmark#via-cli)

Via CLI

    gh workflow run benchmark.yml
    

After the workflow completes, check the **summary** job for a combined comparison table.

These benchmarks run in `SANDBOX_CODE_ONLY` mode. This does **not** represent the performance of Activepieces Cloud, which uses a different sandboxing mechanism to support multi-tenancy. For more information, see [Sandboxing](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/workers#sandboxing)
.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/install/architecture/benchmark.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/install/architecture/benchmark)

[Engine](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/engine)

# Truncated Logs - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/truncated-logs#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Troubleshooting

Truncated Logs

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/truncated-logs#overview)
    
*   [How It Works](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/truncated-logs#how-it-works)
    
*   [Known Limitation](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/truncated-logs#known-limitation)
    
*   [Solution](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/truncated-logs#solution)
    

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/truncated-logs#overview)

Overview
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you see `(truncated)` in the flow run logs, it means the logs have exceeded the maximum allowed file size.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/truncated-logs#how-it-works)

How It Works
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There is a current limitation where the log file of a run cannot grow past a certain size. When this limit is reached, the engine automatically removes the largest keys in the JSON output until it fits within the allowed size.

**This does not affect flow execution.** Your flow will continue to run normally even when logs are truncated.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/truncated-logs#known-limitation)

Known Limitation
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There is one known issue with truncated logs: If you **pause** a flow, then **resume** it, and the resumed step references data from a truncated step, the flow will fail because the referenced data is no longer available in the logs.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/truncated-logs#solution)

Solution
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can increase the `AP_MAX_FILE_SIZE_MB` environment variable to a higher value to allow larger log files:

    AP_MAX_FILE_SIZE_MB=50
    

**Future Improvement:** There is a planned enhancement to change this limit from per-log-file to per-step, which will provide more granular control over log sizes. This feature is currently in the planning phase.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/install/troubleshooting/truncated-logs.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/install/troubleshooting/truncated-logs)

[Reset Password](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/reset-password)
[Websocket Issues](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/websocket-issues)

⌘I

# Deployment Checklist - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/configuration/overview#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Configuration

Deployment Checklist

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

This tutorial assumes you have already followed the quick start guide using one of the installation methods listed in [Install Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
.

In this section, we will go through the checklist after using one of the installation methods and ensure that your deployment is production-ready.

Decide on Sandboxing

You should decide on the sandboxing mode for your deployment based on your use case and whether it is multi-tenant or not. Here is a simplified way to decide:

**Friendly Tip #1**: For multi-tenant setups, use V8/Code Sandboxing.It is secure and does not require privileged Docker access in Kubernetes. Privileged Docker is usually not allowed to prevent root escalation threats.

**Friendly Tip #2**: For single-tenant setups, use No Sandboxing. It is faster and does not require privileged Docker access.

| Name | Supports NPM in Code Piece | Requires Docker to be Privileged | Performance | Secure for Multi Tenant | Reusable Workers | Environment Variable |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| V8/Code Sandboxing | ❌   | No  | Fast & Lightweight | ✅   | ✅   | Set `AP_EXECUTION_MODE` to `SANDBOX_CODE_ONLY` |
| No Sandboxing | ✅   | No  | Fast & Lightweight | ❌   | ✅   | Set `AP_EXECUTION_MODE` to `UNSANDBOXED` |
| Kernel Namespaces Sandboxing | ✅   | Yes | Slow & CPU Intensive | ✅   | ❌   | Set `AP_EXECUTION_MODE` to `SANDBOX_PROCESS` |
| Combined Sandboxing | ❌   | Yes | Medium & CPU Intensive | ✅   | ✅   | Set `AP_EXECUTION_MODE` to `SANDBOX_CODE_AND_PROCESS` |

More Information at [Sandboxing & Workers](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/architecture/workers#sandboxing)

Enterprise Edition (Optional)

For licensing inquiries regarding the self-hosted enterprise edition, please reach out to `[[email protected]](https://www.activepieces.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection) `, as the code and Docker image are not covered by the MIT license.

You can request a trial key from within the app or in the cloud by filling out the form. Alternatively, you can contact sales at [https://www.activepieces.com/sales](https://www.activepieces.com/sales)
.  
Please know that when your trial runs out, all enterprise [features](https://www.activepieces.com/pricing)
 will be shut down meaning any user other than the platform admin will be deactivated, and your private pieces will be deleted, which could result in flows using them to fail.

Before version 0.73.0, you cannot switch from CE to EE directly We suggest upgrading to 0.73.0 with the same edition first, then switch `AP_EDITION`.

Enterprise edition must use `PostgreSQL` as the database backend and `Redis` as the Queue System.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/configuration/overview#installation)

Installation
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Set the `AP_EDITION` environment variable to `ee`.
2.  Set the `AP_EXECUTION_MODE` to anything other than `UNSANDBOXED`, check the above section.
3.  Once your instance is up, activate the license key by going to **Platform Admin -> Setup -> License Keys**. ![Activation License Key](https://mintcdn.com/activepieces/ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP/resources/screenshots/activation-license-key-settings.png?w=2500&fit=max&auto=format&n=ki8mFooo8mAmhMdP&q=85&s=300627457e14ab17abfed9ca7eb8e8f7) 

Setup HTTPS

Setting up HTTPS is highly recommended because many services require webhook URLs to be secure (HTTPS). This helps prevent potential errors.To set up SSL, you can use any reverse proxy. For a step-by-step guide, check out our example using [Nginx](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/guides/setup-ssl)
.

Troubleshooting (Optional)

If you encounter any issues, check out our [Troubleshooting](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/websocket-issues)
 guide.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/install/configuration/overview.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/install/configuration/overview)

[Elestio](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/options/elestio)
[Environment Variables](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/configuration/environment-variables)

# How to handle Requests - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Customer Support

How to handle Requests

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Ticket fields](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#ticket-fields)
    
*   [Requests](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#requests)
    
*   [Type 1: Quick Fixes & Urgent Issues](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#type-1-quick-fixes-%26-urgent-issues)
    
*   [Type 2: Complex Technical Issues](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#type-2-complex-technical-issues)
    
*   [Type 3: Feature Enhancement Requests](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#type-3-feature-enhancement-requests)
    
*   [Type 4: Business Case](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#type-4-business-case)
    
*   [Frequently Asked Questions](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#frequently-asked-questions)
    

As a support engineer, you should:

*   Fix the urgent issues (please see the definition below)
*   Open tickets for all non-urgent issues. **(DO NOT INCLUDE ANY SENSITIVE INFO IN ISSUE)**
*   Keep customers updated
*   Write clear ticket descriptions
*   Help the team prioritize work
*   Route issues to the right people

Our support hours are from **8 am to 6 pm New York time (ET)**. Please keep this in mind when communicating response expectations to customers.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#ticket-fields)

Ticket fields

When handling support tickets, ensure you set the appropriate status and priority to help with ticket management and response time:

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#requests)

Requests

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#type-1-quick-fixes-&-urgent-issues)

Type 1: Quick Fixes & Urgent Issues

*   Understand the issue and how urgent it is.
*   Open a ticket for on linear with “require attention” label and assign someone.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#type-2-complex-technical-issues)

Type 2: Complex Technical Issues

*   Assess the issue and determine its urgency.
*   Always create a Linear issue for the feature request, and send it to the customer.
*   Leave a comment on the Linear issue with an estimated completion time.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#type-3-feature-enhancement-requests)

Type 3: Feature Enhancement Requests

*   Always create a Linear issue for the feature request and send it to the customer.
*   Evaluate the request and dig deeper into what the customer is trying to solve, then either evaluate and open a new ticket or append to an existing ticket in the backlog.
*   Add it to our roadmap and discuss it with the team.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#type-4-business-case)

Type 4: Business Case

*   These cases involve purchasing new features, billing, or discussing agreements.
*   Change the Team to “Success” on Pylon.
*   Tag someone from the Success Team to handle it.

New features will always have the status “Backlog”. Please make sure to communicate that we will discuss and address it in future production cycles so the customer doesn’t expect immediate action.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests#frequently-asked-questions)

Frequently Asked Questions

What if I don't understand the feature or issue?

If you don’t understand the feature or issue, reach out to the customer for clarification. It’s important to fully grasp the problem before proceeding. You can also consult with your team for additional insights.

How do I prioritize multiple urgent issues?

When faced with multiple urgent issues, assess the impact of each on the customer and the system. Prioritize based on severity, number of affected users, and potential risks. Communicate with your team to ensure alignment on priorities.

What if there is an angry or abusive customer?

If you encounter an abusive or rude customer, escalate the issue to Mohammad AbuAboud or Ashraf Samhouri. It’s important to handle such situations with care and ensure that the customer feels heard while maintaining a respectful and professional demeanor.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/handbook/customer-support/handle-requests)

[How to use Pylon](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/pylon)
[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/overview)

⌘I

# Our Compensation - Activepieces

[Skip to main content](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/hiring/compensation#content-area)

[Activepieces home page![light logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/light.svg)![dark logo](https://mintlify.s3.us-west-1.amazonaws.com/activepieces/resources/logo/dark.svg)](https://www.activepieces.com/)

Search...

⌘K

Search...

Navigation

Hiring

Our Compensation

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

The packages include three factors for the salary:

*   **Role**: The specific position and responsibilities of the employee.
*   **Location**: The geographical area where the employee is based.
*   **Level**: The seniority and experience level of the employee.

Salaries are fixed and based on levels and seniority, not negotiation. This ensures fair pay for everyone.

Salaries are updated based on market trends and the company’s performance. It’s easier to justify raises when the business is great.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/handbook/hiring/compensation.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/handbook/hiring/compensation)

[Our Team Structure](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/hiring/team)
[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/overview)

The playbooks are private, Please ask your team for access.

Our infrastructure stack includes several key components to monitor, deploy, and manage our services effectively.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/infrastructure#hosting-providers)

Hosting Providers
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We use two main hosting providers:

*   **DigitalOcean**: Hosts our databases including Redis and PostgreSQL.
*   **Hetzner**: Provides the machines that run our services.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/infrastructure#environments)

Environments
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

| Environment | Domain | Kamal Config |
| --- | --- | --- |
| Staging | `stg.activepieces.com` | `mrsk/stg` |
| Production | `cloud.activepieces.com` | `mrsk/prod` |

Staging receives every merge to `main` and is promoted to production daily at 9 AM UTC. See the [Releases & Deployment](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/releases)
 playbook for the full flow.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/infrastructure#observability-logs-&-telemetry)

Observability: Logs & Telemetry
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We collect logs and telemetry from all services using **HyperDX**.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/infrastructure#kamal-for-deployment)

Kamal for Deployment
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We use **Kamal** as a deployment tool to deploy our Docker containers to staging and production with zero downtime. Kamal configs live on the devops machine under `mrsk/stg` and `mrsk/prod`.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/handbook/engineering/playbooks/infrastructure.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/handbook/engineering/playbooks/infrastructure)

Customer Support

Tone & Communication

[Overview](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/overview/welcome)
[Admin Guide](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/admin-guide/guides/structure-projects)
[Deploy](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/overview)
[Embedding](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/embedding/overview)
[Build Pieces](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/build-pieces/building-pieces/overview)
[API Reference](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/endpoints/overview)
[Handbook](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/overview)

On this page

*   [Casual](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/tone#casual)
    
*   [Fast](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/tone#fast)
    
*   [Honest](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/tone#honest)
    
*   [Always Communicate the Next Step](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/tone#always-communicate-the-next-step)
    
*   [Use “we,” not “I”](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/tone#use-%E2%80%9Cwe%E2%80%9D-not-%E2%80%9Ci%E2%80%9D)
    

Our customers are fellow engineers and great people to work with. This guide will help you understand the tone and communication style that reflects Activepieces’ culture in customer support.

#### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/tone#casual)

Casual

Chat with them like you’re talking to a friend. There’s no need to sound like a robot. For example:

*   ✅ “Hey there! How can I help you today?”
*   ❌ “Greetings. How may I assist you with your inquiry?”
*   ✅ “No worries, we’ll get this sorted out together!”
*   ❌ “Please hold while I process your request.”

#### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/tone#fast)

Fast

Reply quickly! People love fast responses. Even if you don’t know the answer right away, let them know you’ll get back to them with the information. This is the fastest way to make customers happy; everyone likes to be heard.

#### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/tone#honest)

Honest

Explain the issue clearly, don’t be defensive, and be honest. We’re all about open source and transparency here – it’s part of our culture. For example:

*   ✅ “I’m sorry, I forgot to follow up on this. Let’s get it sorted out now.”
*   ❌ “I apologize for the delay; there were unforeseen circumstances.”

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/tone#always-communicate-the-next-step)

Always Communicate the Next Step

Always clarify the next step, such as whether the ticket will receive an immediate response or be added to the backlog for team discussion.

#### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/handbook/customer-support/tone#use-%E2%80%9Cwe%E2%80%9D-not-%E2%80%9Ci%E2%80%9D)

Use “we,” not “I”

*   ✅ “We made a mistake here. We’ll fix that for you.”
*   ❌ “I’ll look into this for you.”
*   You’re speaking on behalf of the company in every email you send.
*   Use “we” to show customers they have the whole team’s support.

Customers are real people who want to talk to real people. Be yourself, be helpful, and focus on solving their problems!

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/handbook/customer-support/tone.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/handbook/customer-support/tone)

Troubleshooting

Queues Dashboard

On this page

*   [Setup BullBoard](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#setup-bullboard)

*   [EXECUTE\_TRIGGER\_HOOK](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#execute-trigger-hook)
    

The Bull Board is a tool that allows you to check issues with scheduling and internal flow runs issues. ![BullBoard Overview](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/felixmosh/bull-board/master/screenshots/overview.png)

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#setup-bullboard)

Setup BullBoard
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To enable the Bull Board UI in your self-hosted installation:

1.  Define these environment variables:
    *   `AP_QUEUE_UI_ENABLED`: Set to `true`
    *   `AP_QUEUE_UI_USERNAME`: Set your desired username
    *   `AP_QUEUE_UI_PASSWORD`: Set your desired password
2.  Access the UI at `/api/ui`

For cloud installations, please ask your team for access to the internal documentation that explains how to access BullBoard.

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#queue-overview)

Queue Overview
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

We have one main queue called `workerJobs` that handles all job types. Each job has a `jobType` field that tells us what it does:

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#low-priority-jobs)

Low Priority Jobs

#### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#renew-webhook)

RENEW\_WEBHOOK

Renews webhooks for pieces that have webhooks channel with expiration like Google Sheets.

#### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#execute-polling)

EXECUTE\_POLLING

Checks external services for new data at regular intervals.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#medium-priority-jobs)

Medium Priority Jobs

#### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#execute-flow)

EXECUTE\_FLOW

Runs flows when they’re triggered.

#### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#execute-webhook)

EXECUTE\_WEBHOOK

Processes incoming webhook requests that start flow runs.

#### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#delayed-flow)

DELAYED\_FLOW

Runs flows that were scheduled for later, like paused flows or delayed executions.

### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#high-priority-jobs)

High Priority Jobs

#### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#execute-property)

EXECUTE\_PROPERTY

Loads dynamic properties for pieces that need them at runtime.

#### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#execute-extract-piece-information)

EXECUTE\_EXTRACT\_PIECE\_INFORMATION

Gets information about pieces when they’re being installed or set up.

#### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#execute-validation)

EXECUTE\_VALIDATION

Checks that flow settings, inputs, or data are correct before running.

#### 

[​](https://www.activepieces.com/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard#execute-trigger-hook)

EXECUTE\_TRIGGER\_HOOK

Runs special logic before or after triggers fire.

Failed jobs are not normal and need to be checked right away to find and fix what’s causing them. They require immediate investigation as they represent executions that failed for unknown reasons that could indicate system issues.

Delayed jobs represent either paused flows scheduled for future execution, upcoming polling job iterations, or jobs being retried due to temporary failures. They indicate an internal system error occurred and the job will be retried automatically according to the backoff policy.

[Suggest edits](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/edit/main/docs/install/troubleshooting/bullboard.mdx)
[Raise issue](https://github.com/activepieces/activepieces/issues/new?title=Issue%20on%20docs&body=Path:%20/install/troubleshooting/bullboard)
